Economic Industry Discussions

— Edited by Tang Qingzeng

Living Standards and Living Expenses (Continued) Zhao Ren

If living standards remain unchanged, fluctuations in living expenses are due to fluctuations in the prices of various items within the standard. If living standards also change, the fluctuations in living expenses become more complex. If standards are reduced while prices rise, living expenses may rise or remain the same. If standards rise while prices fall, expenses may fall or not fall. If standards are reduced and prices also fall, expenses will definitely decrease. If standards rise and prices also rise, expenses will greatly increase. Therefore, those studying living expenses must specify a certain living standard, assuming it remains constant, and observe the level of living expenses based on the rise and fall of prices at different times and places. German statistician Ernst Engel analyzed the income and expenditure of European working-class families in 1857. He first divided the items included in the living standard into five major categories: food, clothing, housing, heating and lighting, and miscellaneous items. Miscellaneous items included education, religion, tuition, health insurance, sports, and entertainment. He then analyzed the distribution of household expenses based on the amount of their income. There were four main conclusions: First, the more income, the smaller the percentage of expenditure on food. Second, the more income, there is no significant increase or decrease in the percentage of expenditure on clothing. Third, regardless of income level, the percentage of expenses for rent, heating, and lighting remains constant. Fourth, the more income, the larger the percentage of total living expenses spent on miscellaneous items such as education, health, and entertainment. Following Engel, sociologists and statisticians from various countries have conducted hundreds of such investigations. Sweden even conducts nationwide household living expense surveys on a regular basis by law. In Shanghai, China, the report of the National Tariff Commission of the Ministry of Finance (formerly the Price Investigation Office in Shanghai) was the first large-scale study on the living expenses of workers, followed by the Shanghai Municipal Bureau of Social Affairs. Their conclusions regarding food and miscellaneous items were completely consistent with Engel's first and fourth points. Clothing expenses showed a significant increase in percentage with the increase in income. The percentage of total living expenses accounted for by rent, heating, and lighting showed a decrease with the increase in income. This kind of research can not only indicate the living conditions and affluence of workers, but also indicate the impact of price changes and the weight of taxes on the material life of workers. If we can study the living standards and expenses of various occupational groups, the dynamics of the national economy can be clearly understood. However, in any country, most of these surveys are still limited to workers, because the survey work is easier, the cost is lower, and workers also occupy the most important position in industrial countries.

In addition to investigating the living conditions of workers, the National Tariff Commission and the Shanghai Municipal Bureau of Social Affairs also compiled a worker living expense index, which was announced monthly. This index first assumes a certain type of worker family, limits its number of people, and assumes that the quantity and quality of the items consumed remain unchanged. Several items are selected as representatives of living expenses, and their market prices are surveyed monthly. At the same time, the importance of these items in the living standard is considered, and a comprehensive average is calculated. For comparison, the prices of each month are first divided by the prices of the same items in a certain period to convert them into percentages, and then a comprehensive average is calculated. Or the comprehensive expenses of each month are divided by the comprehensive expenses of a certain period to find its percentage. This percentage represents the rise and fall of worker living expenses in each month of the year compared with a certain period. For example, the Tariff Commission used 1926 as the basic comparison period. In 1932, the cost of living was 126 percent. This assumes that the worker's living standard remains unchanged. Items that only cost 100 yuan in 1926 would cost 126 yuan in 1932. The index for each month of this year has continued to fall, from 111 percent in January to 104 percent in October. Assuming that the worker's living standard remains unchanged and income remains unchanged, living expenses have clearly decreased in these months. In other words, life should be more comfortable than before. However, the fall in living expenses is due to the fall in prices, and the fall in prices is detrimental to industry and commerce, which may require reduced working hours or factory shutdowns. Workers' income may not be unaffected. Therefore, the rise and fall of living expenses may be a blessing or a disaster for workers, which cannot be arbitrarily determined. If the cost of living falls and income increases or remains the same, workers are more comfortable than before. If the cost of living rises and income falls or remains the same, workers will definitely feel difficulties. Or the cost of living and income fall at the same time, but the former is more severe than the latter, which is good for workers. If the cost of living and income rise at the same time, but the former is more common than the latter, it is a disaster for workers. Rising living expenses indirectly lead to workers demanding increased wages. Or stipulating a minimum wage, using living expenses as a measuring tool, is the reason for this.

Page 7

Pessimistic Outlook for Naval Conference "Four Against One" to Deal with Japan Japan Firmly Opposes Ship Construction Notification Plan England, America, France, and Italy Said to Have Reached an Agreement

London As of this afternoon, the general public is quite pessimistic about the future of the naval conference. It is widely rumored that if Japan still firmly opposes other countries' proposals, causing the naval conference to fail, and the country then greatly increases its naval armaments, then England, France, Italy, and the United States intend to conclude a four-nation agreement to deal with the situation. This agreement will contain a "step-by-step" clause (that is, if countries other than the four signatories increase their naval tonnage, then the four countries can increase their navies according to the same ratio). Naval figures here believe that the proposal to sign a four-nation agreement, with the exception of England, the other three national delegations will all express their approval. Britain is eager for the naval conference to continue working, and no price is too high. It is also generally believed that the British delegation is prepared to study any plan that can extend the conference time, such as discussing political issues. (Havas dispatch on the 7th)

Tokyo It is reported that at the Disarmament Conference Committee on the afternoon of the 8th, the United States attached certain conditions and agreed to the French proposal. England, America, France, and Italy will deal with Japan on a united front. However, the Japanese naval authorities have the following views on the ship construction plan declaration:

The United Kingdom believes that when the quantitative and qualitative restrictions fail to reach an agreement, it proposes a ship construction plan notification case, hoping to reach an agreement, and therefore agrees to the French and Italian proposals, so there is a great possibility of relying on a common battle line. However, the suggestion, as its name suggests, is only a notification of the plan and has no actual restrictions, so it seems to have a deeper meaning. It is necessary to be highly vigilant against those who adhere to such a conciliatory attitude. If it is a countermeasure against other countries' forces, it should be strictly kept secret, but if it is published in advance, no matter how famous the case is, it will lose its secrecy and effectiveness, so it is extremely detrimental to naval countries in an inferior position. The focus of the United Kingdom is here, and France also focuses on Germany, so its true intention is not to promote the spirit of disarmament, nor is its purpose to reserve a place for future disarmament conferences, so it cannot agree to the proposal. (Allied News Agency dispatch on the 8th)

Contents of French and Italian Proposals

London The French delegation to the naval conference suggested yesterday that a naval agreement be established based on the principle of exchanging information on shipbuilding procedures among various naval countries. Italy also made a suggestion based on this principle. The naval delegations of the five countries met separately this afternoon to study the suggestions made by France and Italy. According to inquiries from this agency, the main points of the French proposal are that each naval country must notify each other of the shipbuilding process within one year in advance. If there are difficulties, they should consult with each other, but the information exchanged between countries does not have to be of a general nature and include long-term shipbuilding procedures. According to the British delegation, the French proposal also contains a possibility, that is, the shipbuilding procedures of various countries should be adapted to their construction capabilities, but it is not yet known on what basis this kind of differential treatment is based. As for the Italian proposal, it also advocates that countries notify each other of the shipbuilding process within one year, but there are no regulations on whether to continue exchanging information after one year. (Havas dispatch on the 7th)

Japan Alone Holds Different Views

London According to British naval sources, the suggestions made by Italy and France are very similar. If there is a possibility of reaching a compromise, the United Kingdom will strive to reconcile the views of Italy and France so that they are closer to each other. The main key at present is the attitude of the United States and Japan. The United States believes that Japan should express its opinion first, and then the US delegation can express its position. On this point, the Japanese government spokesman issued a declaration this morning criticizing the French proposal. There are two points of dissent: The French proposal did not stipulate a way to reduce naval armaments, and did not actually recognize the equal rights that Japan demanded. France advocates that shipbuilding procedures should be adapted to the construction capabilities of each country, in other words, shipbuilding should be limited by budgetary capabilities, which is especially harmful to Japan. As far as naval officials know, there is one point that Japan also opposes, but it is inconvenient to formally propose, that is, once the French proposal is implemented, Japan's powerful secret military equipment will inevitably have nowhere to hide. If so, the Japanese navy is not only weaker than the United Kingdom and the United States in terms of quantity, but also inferior in terms of quality, which Japan cannot accept. (Havas dispatch on the 7th)

London The Japanese government spokesman issued a declaration this morning criticizing the French proposal to the naval conference. French delegation officials were very surprised, saying that the outline of the French proposal was only submitted to the delegations of various countries this morning, and the detailed program has not yet been released. The Japanese criticism seems premature. (Havas dispatch on the 7th)

British Press Observations Naval Conference Achievements Unlikely

London Various newspapers have recently commented on the future of the naval conference. Except for the Morning Post, which expressed optimism, the Daily Telegraph and the Japanese People's Voice both issued pessimistic tones. The Morning Post said, "According to the French proposal, each naval country should announce its shipbuilding procedures within one year. In this way, one of the biggest problems of the naval conference, namely the issue of quantitative restrictions, should be resolved as a result." As for the Daily Telegraph, it said, "France advocates that countries exchange information on shipbuilding procedures, but what is announced is only the tonnage, speed, and gun position of the ships to be built. As for the details of the combat power of each ship, which have always been regarded as top secrets by countries, they still cannot be released." The Daily People's Voice reported, "The naval conference is now caught in a storm, and the date of its overturning is not far away. A stalemate is unavoidable after this. The delegations of various countries have tried their best to overcome the difficulties, but they have all failed one after another. This is unavoidable." (Havas dispatch on the 8th)

Comparison of Air Forces of Various Countries

Tokyo Various countries are currently holding disarmament conferences in London to discuss ways to reduce military equipment, but they are separately planning the construction and expansion of various military equipment in their own countries, especially for naval aviation, and they are all devoting their full efforts to enrich their equipment in order to dominate the air in future wars, which is very noteworthy. The current state of enrichment of naval air forces in various countries is roughly as follows:

United States The current number of aircraft is 1,300. When the US Congress reviewed the Vinson shipbuilding plan last year, it decided to grant the navy the authority to increase its aircraft to the number necessary for the naval strength stipulated in the treaty, and limited the maximum number to 2,184. This project plans to manufacture 650 aircraft over five years. In the past year, it has increased 500 crew members to carry out education. When the US Navy launches a fleet attack across the ocean, it is absolutely necessary to first obtain the entire right to dominate the sea where the fleet will fight a decisive battle.

United Kingdom Currently maintains 990 aircraft (among 89 air squadrons, the fleet air force has 13 squadrons, 6 detachments, and 165 aircraft). Last year, it decided on a five-year plan to establish 33 more air squadrons in the country and 8 squadrons in fleet and overseas troops before 1937. According to this plan, the United Kingdom will maintain 2,500 aircraft and increase the number of aviation soldiers from the current 31,000 to 20,000 before 1937.

France The number of aircraft is 1,700 (among 165 squadrons, the naval air force has 53 squadrons and 510 aircraft). The French government started manufacturing 740 aircraft the year before last with a special additional budget of 620 million francs.

Italy The number of aircraft is 1,200 (including 190 naval aircraft). The year before last, it decided on a six-year plan to spend a temporary expenditure of 120 million lira, but last year it was shortened to a three-year plan. The Italian Air Force's heavy bombers can carry more than 1,000 tons of weight, and have a speed of 250 kilometers per hour and a range of 2,000 kilometers, which is extremely powerful.

Germany 2,000 aircraft. Since Hitler declared the reorganization of military equipment, he has been building an air force and plans to expand the number of aircraft to around 3,500.

Soviet Union 2,700 land-based aircraft, 400 sea-based aircraft, for a total of 3,100 aircraft. At the end of last year, it built an aircraft carrier.

Japan The total number of aircraft is 800. The Five-Year Plan will form 3 land-based air squadrons. Before the establishment of the London Treaty, there were 17 squadrons. After the establishment, 14 squadrons were added. In Showa 9, 8 new squadrons were established. The maritime forces have 4 aircraft carriers and 2 seaplane tenders. (Allied News Agency dispatch on the 8th)

Japan Plans to Set Up a Naval Exhibition Hall to Popularize Military Thought Among the Public

Tokyo In order to make the people generally aware of "Japan of the Navy", with the purpose of popularizing naval military thought and cultivating the naval spirit, the Ministry of the Navy plans to build a naval hall with a budget of 450,000 yuan. The construction site is located on a 2,300-ping site on the east side of the Meiji Jingu Outer Garden. A two-story building made of cement and steel will be built. The interior is divided into exhibition rooms, libraries, lecture halls, etc. The exhibition department is divided into modern and historical departments, displaying various models and reference materials. It is heard that the president of the hall will be concurrently held by the Minister of the Navy, and the curator will be a naval official. (Allied News Agency dispatch on the 8th)

British-French Military Mutual Assistance Sea, Land, and Air Cooperation Implemented British and French Experts Complete Plan in Paris The Fleets of the Two Countries Will Conduct Joint Exercises in the Mediterranean

Paris After six weeks of consultation between the staff members of the United Kingdom and France, the plan for the immediate cooperation of the naval, land, and air forces of the two countries has been completed today. If either of the two countries is attacked by another country, the other country will cooperate with all its strength. The military forces of the United Kingdom and France are now prepared to deal with any accidents. Whether the British fleet is attacked at sea in the Mediterranean, or the French border adjacent to Germany, Austria, and Italy is attacked by land, the two countries are very cautious. It is explained that this cooperation is not a secret military alliance, but only a technical preparation. According to the obligation of mutual assistance stipulated in the League of Nations, it is to deal with all accidents. France has designated arsenals, ports, and airports for the British army to use in France, and at the same time, the United Kingdom has also prepared to take on the responsibility of protecting the main coastal cities of France. It is reported that the British army will also assist the French army in defending the forts on the border. (National Telegram on the 7th)

Paris The French military authorities refuse to disclose the results of the British-French staff headquarters meeting. The authorities only said that the recent discussions were "ordinary exchanges of views made by experts from the two countries in a friendly manner." A French external spokesman told reporters that the United Kingdom and France, in accordance with Article 16, Paragraph 3 of the League of Nations, were studying the possibility of cooperation between the two countries in order to resist public enemies. (National Telegram on the 8th)

Paris When the League of Nations' Committee of Eighteen meets in Geneva on January 20 to discuss the oil embargo against Italy, the French First and Second Squadrons will hold large-scale exercises in the Mediterranean. The First Squadron plans to train off the coasts of Provence and Corsica, and the Second Squadron first plans to cruise outside Gaza and Blanca, and then meet with the First Squadron. It is now believed that this exercise is the result of France's repeated commitment to assist the British Mediterranean fleet if it is attacked by Italy. At the same time, the captains of each ship of the Second Squadron will gather in Bress today to talk about war on paper, and they will discuss the strategic issue of what to do if the Second Squadron is attacked before setting off for Gaza and Blanca on January 14. In addition, the battleship "Hotspur" and the cruisers "Leander", "Orion", and "Neptune" will sail back to their home countries from the Mediterranean. (Havas dispatch on the 8th)

Concern About the Outbreak of War Greece Devotes Efforts to National Defense Army Minister's Clear Statement

Athens Today, Army Minister Barboglis clearly stated in the "Anserbos" newspaper the attitude that Greece should take if a European war breaks out. "The European atmosphere is very tense, and no one dares to be sure that the great powers can find a peaceful solution. We absolutely hope for peace. It is certainly not right to say that Greece has no military preparations at all. It is also wrong to say that Greece is engaged in war preparations day and night. British General Staff Advocates Implementing Oil Embargo Against Italy Believes It Is the Only Good Way to Stop the War

Paris According to the "Observer" newspaper's London dispatch today, the British General Staff believes that implementing an oil embargo is a good way to stop the Italian-Abyssinian war. The General Staff also believes that the Italian-Abyssinian conflict must be stopped for the following reasons: If the war is prolonged, the Italian army will eventually suffer significant losses. If blacks win over whites in the war, its adverse effects on colonial countries will be very significant. As far as England is concerned, it will increase the national movements in Egypt, Palestine, and India. To preserve the balance of power in Europe, Italy's power in Europe should not be reduced. Italy's economic recovery relies heavily on British loans. This economic policy should not be stopped for a day. Therefore, the General Staff urges the British government to advocate an oil embargo. The newspaper also said that the atmosphere in London, Geneva, and Paris is in favor of this proposal, so the League of Nations Council meeting on January 20 will definitely pass this resolution and implement it on February 1. (National Telegram on the 7th)

Geneva Tonight, before the League of Nations meets to discuss the oil embargo against Italy, all parties declare that the British General Staff is the most hopeful for the speedy end of the Italian-Abyssinian war. It is said that the best way to stop the war is to cut off Italy's military supplies, and it is appropriate to cut off the supply of oil, cotton, and ammunition, gradually making it feel the shortage of important supplies. The French authorities believe that the United Kingdom's attitude is now constrained by the increasingly serious riots in Egypt, and they also have to take into account the alliance between Germany and Italy. At the same time, experts here are convinced that the oil embargo will not be implemented before February 1, because they must wait for the United States to make a concrete decision on its neutrality policy. (National Telegram on the 7th)

No Progress in the Afghan War; Italy to Increase Troops in East Africa; Two Divisions of Famous Mountain Troops Await Dispatch; Government Orders Conscription of New Soldiers

He has urged the Italian forces in East Africa to intensify their operations simultaneously on both the northern and southern fronts. He has also ordered a newly mobilized division of 17,000 soldiers to immediately depart for East Africa. Furthermore, he has sent the Undersecretary of the Air Force, Fan Er, to Asmara to inspect the air force on the northern front. Foreign military observers here believe that Mussolini's expanded operational plan indicates an imminent renewed effort to seize territory, or to acquire a corridor connecting the Italian territories of Eritrea and Somalia, as this corridor is one of the peace terms proposed by Mussolini. (National Telegram, 7th)

Rome: The Italian government is now conscripting new soldiers to replenish the troops fighting in East Africa. Two orders were issued today: one ordering the formation of a new infantry division to join the six divisions approved last year, and another ordering the formation of an artillery division. The new infantry division is mainly to replenish the Alpine troops departing from Naples to East Africa tonight. The second order mandates the formation of security Blackshirt units to replenish the Blackshirt divisions sent to East Africa. This order is retroactive to February 15, 1935. These units will be assisted by regular army officers. Retired soldiers, except for those in the air force and special units, are eligible to enlist. (Reuters Telegram, 7th)

Rome: The famous mountain troops, known as the "凡爾比斯特利亞" Division, will be completely dispatched to East Africa within days. Yesterday, several battalions of this division, totaling 4,000 infantry and artillery soldiers, departed first aboard the mail ship "康特衫蘭特". Tonight, another battalion will depart from the port of Naples on the ship "康特羅沙" for the front. Both ships are the largest and newest type of Italian merchant vessels. This is the first time they have been used to transport troops to East Africa. Other units will be transported to East Africa on the mail ship "意大利" on the 9th of this month. In addition, a division of mountain light infantry has now been concentrated at the port of Naples and will also depart from there within days to strengthen the forces in East Africa. Once these two divisions have fully departed, the number of regular Italian troops sent to East Africa since the start of the war will reach seven divisions. This does not include six divisions of Fascist Blackshirts and several divisions of local indigenous troops. The most recently established of these indigenous troops is the "利比亞" Division, which was formed yesterday in the Italian port of Tripoli. The Governor-General of Libya, General Balbo, personally conducted the flag presentation ceremony. One side of the flag bears the Italian tricolor national emblem, while the other side is green, symbolizing the unity and cooperation between Italy and Islam. The government has recently ordered the mobilization of the "哥西里亞" and "亞細亞泰" divisions, intending to send them to Libya immediately to increase the number of domestic troops there to four divisions. (Havas, 7th)

World Oil Production Statistics for October Last Year

Increased Production in the United States; German Company and Italian Merchant Agree to Contract

Geneva: The League of Nations recently released the crude oil production figures for various countries around the world for October of last year, totaling 19,362,000 tons. Compared with the 16,249,000 tons in February of last year and the 17,807,000 tons in October 1934, this figure is the highest since the League of Nations began publishing these statistics. Among the oil-producing countries in the world, the United States has increased production the most, from only 10,505,000 tons in October of the year before last to 12,087,000 tons in October of last year. (Havas, 7th)

After the US Agricultural Adjustment Act Became Invalid, the Secretary of Agriculture Convened a National Leaders' Meeting; Production Controls Continued as Usual

Washington: President Roosevelt met with reporters today and stated that he would ask Congress to appropriate funds to pay farmers who had signed production restriction contracts under the Agricultural Adjustment Act in 1935. However, the President did not directly answer the question of the Supreme Court's ruling that the Act was invalid. The reporters asked three questions: What is the government's current rural plan? Will there be any legislation related to rural areas passed during this session of Congress? If Congress approves the requested appropriation, what kind of new tax will the government levy? The President repeatedly replied to these three questions, "There is no news on this point." (National Telegram, 7th)

Washington: Secretary of Agriculture Wallace suddenly gave a radio address today, stating that after the Agricultural Adjustment Act became invalid, the United States would likely face a rural crisis again within a few years. "After the business tax is abolished, the results may be quite good for one or two years, but after this period, the entire rural area of the country will be greatly reduced." Before the speech, Wallace had invited agricultural leaders from across the country to come here for a meeting to discuss future plans after the Supreme Court ruling. The meeting is scheduled to open on Friday. (National Telegram, 7th)

Washington: New Deal figures are maintaining a conservative silence regarding yesterday's Supreme Court ruling that the Agricultural Adjustment Act was invalid. However, the White House urgently convened a meeting. After the meeting, it was learned that Congress will be asked to allocate $250,000,000 for farmer welfare expenses already being handled by the government. At the same time, an Associated Press reporter learned that the trend of the Supreme Court's ruling would likely follow one of the following paths: Amendment of the Constitution; equalization fees, export bonds, or domestic distribution plans; separation of progressive taxes and production controls; recommendations to limit the power of the Supreme Court; government subsidies to control food production. Dispatches from New England stated that the textile industry there was overjoyed to hear of the Supreme Court's ruling, and the Cotton Manufacturers Association also believed that it would benefit industry. (National Telegram, 7th)

Washington: The newspapers of the Scripps Howard chain said yesterday's Supreme Court rejection of the Agricultural Adjustment Act was a "resistance war" against Roosevelt and the United States, arguing that Roosevelt had only two paths to follow: to offer no resistance and accept the ruling, limiting all his political actions to the army, navy, and the District of Columbia; or to recognize the provocative action and appeal to the people to gauge public opinion as to whether they wished to be governed by their elected president and Congress, or by this deformed judicial body. These newspapers stated that they did not wish to criticize the ruling, as this court inherently had this power in law. However, the question now is whether the nation wishes to be governed by this judicial oligarchy, which cannot but become a major question. These newspapers further stated that the tyranny of the judiciary is very dangerous, because the judiciary is not subject to the control of popular elections. Finally, the newspapers raised a question: should today's government be a government of the people, by the people, and for the people, or should it be a government ruled by the Supreme Court? (National Telegram, 7th)

Washington: Agricultural Adjustment Administration officials stated today in their private capacity that the cotton public storage agency will not be affected by the court's ruling, as this agency has nothing to do with the processing tax or production controls and will continue as usual. (Reuters Telegram, 6th)

Washington: After the Supreme Court ruled yesterday that the Agricultural Adjustment Act was unconstitutional, 135 representatives of various railway companies have separately petitioned various courts to repeal laws concerning the collection of railway taxes and wage income taxes. Washington: Commerce Department Financial Division Director Jones revealed during a report to the House of Representatives today that the price of one Chinese national currency will not exceed 35 US cents. He also stated that the current price of the Chinese national currency actually depends on the exchange rate between the US dollar and the British pound, because its exchange rate against the British pound does not exceed 1 shilling and 2.5 pence, and the exchange rate between the US dollar and the British pound does not exceed $4.92. Finally, Jones pointed out that after China's national silver management exchange depreciated the currency value, it could save the US Navy $1 million in US dollars when purchasing goods from China. (National Telegram, 7th)

The federal government may be forced to raise $2,583,000,000 to pay farmers' crop restriction subsidies owed by the Agricultural Adjustment Administration. Another inflationary factor is that Congress may pass a bill to pay $220,000,000 in cash for veteran benefits. However, if the courts force the government to return the taxes collected from merchants under the Agricultural Adjustment Act, an even more serious problem will arise. However, the general public believes that this will not happen. Officials are quite wary of this because the possible ruling that the farmer subsidies are illegal has exhausted them. US Authorities Review New Chinese Legislation; Senate Investigates Morgan Silver Company Case

Washington: The House Foreign Affairs Committee recently met and began reviewing the new Chinese Legislation Act proposed by Committee Chairman McClernon. Assistant Secretary of State Mole also attended the meeting. According to McClernon, today's meeting was only preliminary in nature. Tomorrow, the meeting will continue, and the State Department will send experts to attend and provide detailed explanations of the Chinese Legislative Act. International law expert Paul Chue will attend the meeting the day after tomorrow to provide opinions. (Havas, 7th)

Washington: The Senate Arms Investigation Committee met today to examine the case of Morgan Silver Company providing financial assistance to the Entente countries before the United States entered the Great War in 1917. A large number of police officers were stationed around the meeting place to provide security. Banking giants Morgan Lamont and Vanderbilt were summoned to testify. Morgan first stated the situation at the time, saying that Morgan Silver Company, due to Switzerland's violation of Belgium's neutrality and the European situation falling into crisis, feared that if Germany were to win the war, the "world's freedom and rights would be in danger of perishing." In order to avoid this, it decided to provide funds and goods to the Entente countries. He represented the governments of Britain and France in purchasing goods in the United States, with a total value of $3 billion. The commission earned by Morgan Silver Company was 1%, totaling $30 million. The first loan to the Entente countries was in 1915, at which time the Entente countries' finances had fallen into distress, so the loan was provided to help them. As for the Investigation Committee's claim that this loan was the main reason for the United States' entry into the war, it was not true. He always believed that the United States joined the Great War because Germany adopted an unrestricted submarine policy. After Morgan finished his statement, the committee members declared that Morgan's loan to the Entente countries was contrary to the United States' traditional policy of neutrality, which President Wilson had declared in August 1914 when the war broke out. Morgan replied that American banks had expressed sympathy to the Entente countries "since the beginning of the war." Lamont also stood up and stated that "spiritual neutrality is impossible." At this point, the committee members recalled the fact that the French government had borrowed $20 million using treasury bills as collateral, saying that Morgan had refused this loan because it violated the United States' neutral stance. However, not long after, Morgan agreed to purchase French public bonds. Later, in March 1915, when public opinion was favorable to the Entente countries, he organized a silver company to subscribe to as much as $50 million of French bonds, which shows a clear contradiction between the previous and subsequent circumstances. Lamont then said that his aid to the Entente countries was sincere. In 1915, another major American banker, Kuhn Loeb, had proposed lending money to Germany, so Morgan Silver Company quickly assisted France to deal with it. The committee then asked about the relationship between the late President Wilson and Morgan Silver Company, and between the State Department and the silver company. However, Morgan and the other two said that they had a poor memory due to the passage of time. (Havas, 7th)

Radio Image Transmission; Japan to Hold Public Experiments

Beining Railway Funds Intercepted by Yin Rugeng

Large Stations Extract Funds Daily, Small Stations Every Three Days

Tianjin Correspondence: The Beining Railway, from Tanggu eastward to Shanhaiguan, is 317 kilometers long, accounting for four-fifths of the entire Beining Railway trunk line. The puppet Jidong Autonomous Government recently established a puppet Xin Yu Section Railway Supervisory Office in Tangshan. The internal plan of this office was to set up six departments: Transportation, Machinery, Works, Accounting, Police, and General Affairs, to occupy this section of the railway. However, due to the involvement of British loans in the railway and after detailed audits, it was found that if the occupation were implemented, the passenger and freight revenue from Tanggu to Yuguan stations would be at most just over one million yuan per month. This figure is even based on peak months; during slow business periods, at most only 700,000 yuan could be obtained. After deducting expenses, there would be no surplus. Subsequently, with the assistance of a certain foreign railway expert in raising funds, it was decided to avoid the name of occupation and focus on intercepting railway funds. Although the puppet Supervisory Office was established, its internal organization was not ambitious. However, it severely monitored the railway funds of each station east of Tanggu, dispatching puppet troops to assist, forbidding the section chiefs and stationmasters to remit funds to Tianjin, and instead directly extracted the funds through the puppet Supervisory Office. Large stations extracted funds daily, while small stations did so every three days, all of which were sent to the puppet Supervisory Office in Tangshan for safekeeping. Tangshan, Yuguan, Tanggu, and Luanxian have already extracted more than 50,000 yuan in one week. The amount extracted from other small stations has not yet been reported to the railway bureau. Stationmasters and section chiefs are required to prepare two copies of any matters reported to the railway bureau, one submitted to the railway bureau and one submitted to the puppet Supervisory Office for review. When the railway bureau issues orders to each station, the section chiefs and stationmasters must also prepare a copy and send it to the puppet office for inspection. The puppet office has not issued any orders, but it is implementing its puppet supervisory power to prevent the section chiefs and stationmasters from plotting anything detrimental to their side. The Beining Railway Bureau is currently anxious because the puppet organization is intercepting railway funds for a long time, leaving the railway bureau with only expenses and no income. The salaries of all employees and all other expenses will be impossible to maintain. If a solution is not found quickly, not only will austerity measures be necessary, but also preparations must be made to borrow money to maintain future expenses. Therefore, the Jidong issue must be resolved quickly, and the Beining Railway issue must be addressed and the interception of funds stopped as soon as possible. (6th)

Agreement on the Recovery of the Kuling British Concession

Four Supplementary Articles to the Agreement: Old Property Deeds to Be Exchanged for New Ones

Nanchang Correspondence: The agreement on the recovery of the Kuling British Concession was formally signed by Jiang Zhicheng, Director of the Lushan Management Bureau, and the British side on December 30, 1935. The takeover was carried out on New Year's Day this year, and a celebration ceremony was held at 10:00 am that day. More than a thousand people, both Chinese and foreign, attended the ceremony with joy. In the evening, a lantern parade was also held. The agreement consists of 14 articles and 4 supplementary articles. After the recovery, all old property deeds within the area must be returned to the Lushan Management Bureau and exchanged for new deeds issued by the Chinese government. The full text of the agreement and the deed format are recorded below:

Agreement: The Director of the Lushan Management Bureau, authorized by the Jiangxi Provincial Government, and the British Consul-General in Hankou, representing the Kuling Property Board (i.e., the property trustee), and authorized by the board, enter into the following agreement: The British Consul-General, with the approval of the Kuling property owners' meeting on August 11, 1933, with the permission of the Kuling Property Board, agrees to return the lease issued by the Chinese government to Li Delie in 1895 and the extended lease of 1904. The Lushan Management Bureau agrees to issue perpetual leases to the existing property owners of various nationalities within the Kuling property area, the boundaries of which are shown in the map. The exchange of leases shall be handled by the Lushan Management Bureau. Regardless of how ownership has been transferred in the past, the current property owners are recognized as the owners of the property. To facilitate the exchange of leases, the Director of the Lushan Management Bureau may solicit the opinions and assistance of representatives of Kuling property owners. The Land Section of the Lushan Management Bureau shall have the authority to determine land area and boundaries. In case of disputes, the Lushan Management Bureau shall appoint a special commissioner to resolve them. The commissioner shall appoint a special committee with the commissioner as chairman, and Chinese and foreign property owners may each send representatives to participate in the committee. When necessary, based on the Kuling property register, the committee shall have the right to survey the disputed land. When the exchange of leases is completed, Li Delie's lease and the extended lease of 1905 shall be submitted to the Chinese authorities for cancellation. The administration of the current Kuling property shall be transferred to the Lushan Management Bureau or the office or personnel established by the Jiangxi Provincial Government for managing Lushan affairs on January 1 of the year following the signing of this agreement. For the common benefit of the Chinese and foreign residents within the former Kuling property area, the Director of the Lushan Management Bureau shall establish an advisory committee for a period of seven years. On important matters affecting the public welfare of residents within the former Kuling property area, the Director of the Lushan Management Bureau shall consult with the advisory committee. The advisory committee shall be composed of seven property owners within the former Kuling property area, three of whom shall be foreigners nominated by foreign property owners. The advisory committee shall elect two subcommittees from its members: a finance committee and a works committee. Each subcommittee shall have at least one foreign member of the advisory committee. Within the scope of the former Kuling property area, foreigners may transfer their existing perpetual leases, but they must apply to the Lushan Management Bureau for registration of the transfer and pay the prescribed fees. Existing foreign shops are allowed to continue operating within the former Kuling property area, subject to compliance with local municipal regulations and rules. With the agreement of both parties, the Lushan Management Bureau shall accept the assets and liabilities of the Kuling property area. These assets and liabilities, and all associated responsibilities, shall be specified in a certificate issued by a well-known registered accounting firm. All houses and properties owned and managed under trust deeds, and which are not public property of the board, shall continue to be owned and managed by the trust deeds. These deeds shall be respected. Except for schools and cemeteries, this property shall be subject to local taxes. In accordance with Article 11 of this Agreement, the Lushan Management Bureau shall inherit the rights and benefits of managing the various properties enjoyed by the former Kuling Property Board. The Lushan Management Bureau shall publish an annual report, budget, and audited accounts for distribution. A certified copy of this agreement shall be registered with the Ministry of Foreign Affairs and the British Embassy in China. The signing of this agreement is an expression of friendship between the residents of Lushan of all nationalities, and it is hoped that it will promote the situation within the Lushan area.

Supplementary Articles: The signatories of the formal agreement agree to exchange notes on the following points:

Lease Format: (To be determined and attached to the exchange of notes) The lease shall be drafted immediately. The lease shall grant the Lushan Management Bureau the right to enter and dispose of the land parcel in case of unjustified failure to pay various donations and land taxes. Assurances for the tranquility of Lushan, concerning the source of water and forest cultivation, must be respected. A fee of one yuan will be charged for issuing new deeds to each property owner. Acceptance of the certificate issued by the registered accountant, which clearly states the assets and liabilities of the Kuling property.

Deed Format: Lushan Management Bureau, Jiangxi Province, Republic of China

Issuance of Perpetual Lease Deed: Now, according to Mr./Ms. ××× (hereinafter referred to as the perpetual lessee) of × nationality, who has applied for a perpetual lease of land in the Kuling area of Lushan (formerly known as Kuling Section × Land)

Measuring × mu × fen × li × hao (calculated at × English square feet per mu), bounded on the north by ×××, on the south by ×××, on the east by ×××, and on the west by ×××, etc. The perpetual lessee has submitted the old deed to the Lushan Management Bureau of Jiangxi Province and requested the issuance of a perpetual lease deed from the Chinese government, and is willing to pay the land tax levied by the local government of Lushan to the Chinese authorities each year in accordance with the regulations. After verification by this bureau, it is found to be true and has been entered in the register on × year × month × day of the Republic of China, No. ×. Therefore, a perpetual lease deed is hereby issued to the perpetual lessee, who shall manage the land in accordance with the following provisions. If the perpetual lessee or his/her heirs or assignees fail to pay the above-mentioned land tax in advance each year, and fail to comply even after being ordered to pay, this deed shall be considered invalid, and all ownership or all rights and other benefits of the land and the buildings thereon shall revert to the Chinese government. However, the Lushan Management Bureau permits the perpetual lessee to prepay land tax for up to five years.

The perpetual lessee or his/her heirs or assignees shall pay the local taxes and administrative levies assessed by the Lushan Management Bureau or its legal successors or assignees on the perpetual lease property at any time in accordance with the law.

If there are unpaid local taxes and administrative levies, after twelve months from the notice (starting from April 1 or after April 1 each year), and the house has been occupied, or after twenty-four months from the notice, and the house is still unoccupied, the Lushan Management Bureau or its legal successors or assignees have the right to seal off or occupy the perpetual lease land and the buildings thereon and the leasehold benefits until the unpaid taxes and levies are paid and the liabilities are discharged. However, once the unpaid taxes and levies are paid on time, the Lushan Management Bureau shall lift the seal and restore the original property to its original state, and hand it over to the perpetual lessee for free management and enjoyment in accordance with the provisions of the perpetual lease.

The perpetual lessee shall not allow any unclean objects to flow from the house into the streams and waterways passing through the perpetual lease land, and shall not change the streams or waterways or engage in any behavior that may obstruct or pollute the water flow.

The mortgage or transfer of the perpetual lease property and the buildings thereon shall be registered with the Lushan Management Bureau.

The perpetual lessee shall comply with and implement all laws and regulations of the Lushan Management Bureau regarding the property.

Director ××× Date of issuance to the perpetual lessee: × year × month × day of the Republic of China, Deed No. ×

Shandong Tobacco Production Increases

But Value Declines, Many Tobacco Merchants Suffer Losses

Jinan Correspondence: Various counties along the Jiaoji Railway in eastern Shandong are abundant in tobacco production, with tobacco quality superior to that produced in Bengbu and Henan. In addition, it is close to the railway, making transportation convenient, and in previous years it was a major source of income for the region. Not only was it sold to Shanghai, but many tobacco factories in the province also used it. In recent years, tobacco prices have fallen, significantly less than before. Last year's production was more than in previous years. The output of Linzi, Yidu, Weixian, and Anqiu counties have all increased. However, tobacco merchants and small companies have traditionally purchased from farmers before harvest and then resold to large companies. Last year, due to the low tobacco prices, many of those engaged in this business suffered irreparable losses, and some went bankrupt. By the end of the year, most of the Chinese and foreign tobacco companies along the railway had successively stopped weighing tobacco. The total amount collected by each company was more than 660 tons, with a value of about 15 million yuan. The results of the investigation are compared as follows: Yizhong Company (formerly reorganized from the British-American Tobacco Company) purchased the most, over 9 million yuan, averaging 16 yuan per hundred pounds; Linhua Company was second (formerly renamed from the British American Tobacco Company); Huacheng Company had over 1 million yuan; Nanyang Company had several hundred thousand yuan; Mixing had 500,000 yuan; Nanxin had over 200,000 yuan; and the remaining companies had over 1 million yuan. As for the tobacco production locations, Tanjiafangzi, at the border between Shouguang and Changle counties, benefited the most, because the soil is more fertile and the tobacco color is superior. Some sold for over 70 yuan per hundred pounds. The highest income per mu was 260-270 yuan, and the lowest was 70-80 yuan. Weixian was the worst, with the highest income per mu being over 100 yuan, and some earning less than 20 yuan. The reason is mainly due to soil conditions. Some have continuously planted tobacco for 15 years, and the inferior tobacco color is naturally expected. Comparing the export locations, Xindian had the most, with over 1,100 cars transported out via the Jiaoji Railway. Tobacco produced in Linzi, Changshan, and Huantai mostly concentrated here, with a value of 5 million yuan. Tanjiafangzi had 600 cars, worth 3 million yuan; Yidu had 800-900,000 yuan; Yangjiazhuang had 7-800,000 yuan; Weixian had 2-300,000 yuan; Ershilibu had 1 million yuan; Hamatun had 500,000 yuan; Huangqibao had 1 million yuan. However, the value was lower. What used to be 30 yuan per hundred pounds is now only worth 60-70% of that. The companies have now stopped collecting, and many tobacco farmers still have unsold tobacco in storage.

Songjiang County Government Actively Combating Opium

The province is implementing a policy to prohibit opium. Opium smokers holding licenses are being ordered to quit. So far, the county has reached its thirteenth batch. Although many have followed the summons and have surrendered themselves to be cured, many others who used false names when registering for a license have not been found when summoned, and are still addicted. After County Magistrate Li took office, he took opium prohibition as one of the main policies of the province. He could not perfunctorily ignore this, so he issued a list of the names of the opium smokers holding licenses who have been repeatedly summoned but have not been found, or have delayed treatment, to the various district offices, ordering the heads of the bao and jia to investigate and arrest them together with the police officers of the Public Security Bureau. In recent days, various districts have been investigating, arresting, and sending those arrested to the county in many instances. Furthermore, according to a provincial order, in order to be cautious in imprisonment and lenient in punishment, opium smokers who have not obtained a license are allowed to register for self-rehabilitation from January 1 to the end of the month, and be subject to the law. After the deadline, the heads of the bao and jia will report them and they will be punished for private smoking. The heads of the bao and jia must also provide a written guarantee that there are no private smokers within their area. If a private smoker is found after the guarantee, the head of the bao and jia who concealed the fact will also be subject to appropriate punishment. This self-rehabilitation registration was widely publicized last year in December, and the heads of the bao and jia were responsible for investigating, listing, and reporting. Now that the deadline for self-rehabilitation registration is about to expire, the time for the general inspection of opium and drug offenders is approaching. The county's Anti-Opium Committee has followed the order to conduct a general inspection and expanded the publicity, formulating publicity guidelines and distributing them to various districts. The county government has recently convened representatives from various agencies to discuss ways to implement this public awareness campaign.

Nanhui Buying Silver Dollars Punishable by Seven Years

Jiang Liansheng, Chen Miaohong, and Zhang Amao from Shanghai bought silver dollars in Zhoupu Town in this county on October 8 last year. They were seized by the people of the town and sent to the First Sub-Bureau of the Public Security Bureau. 108 silver dollars were found, and they were sent to the county for interrogation and detention. The verdict was handed down on the fourth, and the three defendants were each sentenced to seven years of imprisonment. The 108 silver dollars were confiscated.

Suzhou Private Transportation of Raw Silver Reported to the Province for Instructions

Xia Liben, an employee of the Suzhou Youhuo Bank, went to Zhejiang to collect more than 2,500 taels of raw silver in preparation for transporting it to Shanghai. However, he was found by the police at the Pingwang Town bus station in Wujiang County. Although he had a silver transport passport from the Ministry of Finance, the numbers and dates did not match, and the handwriting on the passport was in both brush and fountain pen. He was deemed to be transporting it privately. The witnesses were also detained and sent to the Wujiang County Government on the seventh for interrogation and detention. County Magistrate Xu of the county believed that Xia Liben was suspected of forging a passport and privately transporting raw silver, in serious violation of the provincial order. On the eighth, he reported the incident to the Jiangsu Provincial Government for instructions.

Wuxi Dozens of Lake Bandits Continuously Rob Farmhouses

The Weijiali area, about three li away from Huadafang Village in the third district of the county, is located on the shore of Taihu Lake. The village is remote, and the residents, such as Zhou Yonggen and Zhou Aquan, are farmers and are doing well. Recently, the new grains have been harvested, which attracted the attention of the bandits. At about 4 o'clock in the morning on the seventh, more than 20 lake bandits suddenly came to the village, driving small boats, each holding pistols, flashlights, short knives, and other weapons. They first went to Zhou Aquan's house, climbed over the walls, and tied up more than a dozen people, young and old, and searched at will. Then they went to Zhou Yonggen's house and tied up the whole family in the same way, allowing them to search. After two hours, they left with their loot. After the incident, the lost items were checked, and it was found that the two families were robbed of more than 30 yuan in legal tender and more than 30 dan of white rice, totaling 4-500 yuan in losses.

Yangzhou County Government Sets Up a Questioning Office for Opium Smokers

The county government has recently started the self-rehabilitation registration for opium smokers. However, because people's knowledge is limited, although proclamations have been issued frequently to explain the registration procedures, it is feared that they may not be able to understand them and miss the opportunity to rehabilitate themselves. Therefore, the county government has stipulated measures for opium smokers to ask questions, ordering district, township, and town offices, bao chiefs' offices, as well as the Public Security Bureau and its various sub-bureaus and teams, to set up self-rehabilitation opium smoker inquiry offices in their respective locations, and to provide detailed explanations to opium smokers who have questions at any time.

Nantong Military Police Search and Suppress Local Bandits in the Southern Countryside

Bandit flags have recently been unstable in Tongyi. According to reports, the Nantong District Commissioner's Office learned that a large group of local bandits was gathering in the southern countryside. On the morning of the seventh, Commissioner Xu Zhen, supervised the security team. The chief of the Public Security Bureau, Song Mingqi, led the police team to Yongxing, Zhuhang, Xingang and other towns to conduct a large-scale search and suppression. Hangzhou Lake Palace Hotel Guest Commits Suicide

Gan Shitian, a young traveler in his twenties, arrived at the Lake Palace Hotel on Yingzi Road in Hangzhou City on the fourth of this month. He checked into room number ten and there was nothing unusual. He suddenly took poison while sleeping with the door closed on the evening of the seventh. At eleven o'clock on the morning of the eighth, the room attendant called but there was no response. Knowing that something was wrong, he opened the door and entered. The guest was lying stiff on the bed and had died. He reported it to the Public Security Bureau, which informed the Hangzhou Local Court to send officials for inspection. The guest's books indicated that he was from Jiangsu Province. He had no money on him. It is presumed that he committed suicide due to economic difficulties.

Ningbo Yuyao Salt Tide Becomes Tense Again

More than 200 salt farmers in the second and third districts of eastern Yuyao gathered at the Xiangong Temple on the morning of the fifth, due to the fact that the four major salt factories in Zhejiang, namely, Dong, Wu, Gong, and Yuantai, have been delaying the purchase of salt, causing them to suffer from hunger and cold. They often sent representatives to inquire at the Gongxing Factory, but they did not receive a satisfactory answer. They took Feng Meiyan, the accountant of the factory, to the Andongchang Office, requesting punishment and urging the factory to speed up the purchase of salt. The head of the field comforted the salt farmers and ordered the accountant, Feng Meiyan, to contact the factory and open it for collection within five days. The salt farmers gradually dispersed upon hearing this. Therefore, the situation in the salt field has become tense again in recent days.

Domestic Exchange Fees Regulations Domestic and Foreign Exchanges are Settled at the BOC Exchange Rate

New Sound News Agency reported that since the implementation of the new currency system policy, domestic exchange has tended to be balanced. The Bankers Association has abolished the Market Committee, and stopped publishing market prices every day from January 4. The Central, China, and Communications Banks have newly formulated domestic exchange handling fee methods, which are recorded as follows: Exchange to other provinces, the fee is one yuan per thousand yuan. Exchange to this province, the fee is five jiao per thousand yuan. For exchanges below one hundred yuan, the minimum fee is one jiao. For exchanges over one hundred yuan, the minimum fee is two jiao. All banks operating domestic exchanges have now handled the above-mentioned methods.

Stable Foreign Exchange: After the Central, China, and Communications Banks bought and sold foreign exchange without restrictions, the foreign exchange market has stabilized. Yesterday morning, the Central Bank's exchange rate for London was one shilling and two and a half pence, and for New York it was twenty-nine US dollars. The exchange rate quoted by HSBC was slightly lower. The Chinese banks that also handled foreign exchange were Zhejiang Xingye, Zhejiang Shiye, Shanghai, Dongya, Kenye, Guohuo, Guohua, Huaqiao, Dalu, Zhongfu, Zhongnan, Zhongxing, Jincheng, and Qiye, totaling fourteen. They are now all settled according to the exchange rate quoted by the Central Bank. Foreign banks are all engaged in foreign exchange, but now, because there is no profit to be made, they have restricted buying and selling.

Private Smuggling Disappears

The Foreign Exchange Equalization Committee announced yesterday morning at ten o'clock that the equalization tax rate was 9%, which was 1.25% higher than yesterday's. In addition, because the method for foreign banks to hand in cash for exchange has been negotiated, foreign silver prices have plummeted. Therefore, those who pay taxes for export and those who smuggle have disappeared.

Construction of the Sichuan-Hunan Highway Hunan Province Signs Loan

Totaling 1.5 Million, Borrowed from Three Banks Payment Due Next Month, Term is Ten Months, Interest is Eight Percent

The Hunan Provincial Government, in order to complete the Sichuan-Hunan Highway, which was lacking funds, sent Yu Jichuan, Director of the Provincial Department of Construction, to Shanghai on the 20th of last month. After contacting Kong Xiangxi, President of the Central Bank, Song Ziwen, Chairman of the Board of Directors of the Bank of China, and Tang Shoumin, General Manager of the Bank of Communications, the banks have agreed to jointly lend 1.5 million yuan. The loan contract has been formally signed. The Central Bank will borrow 600,000 yuan, the Bank of China will borrow 600,000 yuan, and the Bank of Communications will borrow 300,000 yuan, totaling 1.5 million yuan. The remaining construction bonds of 3 million yuan, which were previously mortgaged by Hunan Province, will be used as collateral, and the Hunan Province's land tax revenue will be used as a guarantee for principal and interest. The interest rate is 8%, the term is 10 months, and 150,000 yuan will be repaid each month starting in April 1937. As for the payment method, it will be delivered in February, March, April, and May in the ratio of two, three, four, and five, respectively. 400,000 yuan will be paid monthly for the first three months, and 300,000 yuan will be paid in the fourth month. The first payment is scheduled to be paid directly to the Hunan Provincial Department of Construction by the Changsha branches of the Central, China, and Communications Banks on February 1 in the ratio of 4:4:2.

Last Year, Shanghai Goods Exports to US Increased Sharply, Silver Exports to US Decreased

According to statistics released by the U.S. Consulate General in Shanghai on Thursday, Shanghai's exports to the United States in 1935 were worth US$18,557,026, an increase of US$6,403,261 compared to the total value of US$9,343,801 in 1934. However, exports to the Philippines and Hawaii both decreased slightly. Exports to the Philippines were US$1,146,417, compared to US$1,330,328 in 1934. Exports to Hawaii were US$54,713, compared to US$60,275 in 1934. In 1935, Shanghai's exports to the United States in all categories of goods increased. Inedible plant products increased from US$1,352,993 in 1934 to US$4,960,669 in 1935. Textiles increased from US$4,640,771 in 1934 to US$6,396,968 in 1935. Edible animals and animal products increased significantly, from US$85,201 in 1934 to US$814,844 in 1935. In 1935, the amount of silver shipped from Shanghai to the United States decreased significantly. In 1934, 43,518,901 ounces were shipped, worth a total of US$19,657,378. In 1935, this decreased to 115,500 ounces, worth a total of US$58,424. The silver sold to American banks by the National Government at the end of 1935 and the beginning of this year and shipped out was apparently not included in these figures.

French Municipal Council Approves Telephone Price Increase

The issue of Shanghai Telephone Company's telephone price increase has recently been resolved in the French Concession. It is said that it has been decided to implement it in the French Concession starting from March 1st this year. The French Shanghai Daily, translated by the Foreign News Agency, records the following:

According to the French Concession Municipal Council, the official acceptance of the telephone price increase was actually decided at the board meeting on December 30, 1935. The reasons for the acceptance are threefold: The number of telephones in the French Concession is relatively small, so opposing the price increase would not be able to withstand the pressure of the majority in the Public Concession. The Shanghai Municipal Council in the Public Concession has publicly accepted and announced it. If the French Concession authorities were to oppose it alone, it would undermine the unity of all foreign groups. The review report of the French Concession on the telephone price increase is largely the same as the review report of the Public Concession. For these reasons, the Municipal Council decided to accept the Shanghai Municipal Council and decided to implement the price increase in both concessions simultaneously from March 1, 1936. However, the French Concession Municipal Council has several reservations attached to the acceptance of the price increase: The money paid by the Shanghai Telephone Company to the International Telephone and Telegraph Corporation. The operating expenses of the company's New York office. The income tax levied on the company by the U.S. government. The above three items were not originally within the scope of the patent agreement, so the company should list them separately for future research when revising telephone charges. In addition, the French Concession Municipal Council also urged the telephone company to pay attention to improving the costs incurred in installing and repairing automatic machines, etc. Since the French Concession Municipal Council agreed to the telephone price increase, the price increase will be implemented on March 1st. The price increase method is as follows: Shops: 10 yuan per month, limited to 150 calls. Each additional call will be charged 3 cents. Private residences: 6.5 yuan per month, limited to 100 calls. Each additional call will be charged 3 cents. Extension fee: 6 yuan per month.

Dalu Daily reports that the French Concession Municipal Council held a special meeting on December 30 last year and approved the Shanghai Municipal Council's resolution to charge telephone fees per call. It will formally notify the Shanghai Telephone Company of this within a few days. At the same time, the French Concession Municipal Council has several points that are not yet clear regarding the basis for calculating the fees, so it made certain reservations when approving the charging per call. In addition, the French Concession Municipal Council needs to investigate the past and present costs of installing, repairing, and maintaining automatic telephone exchanges from an economic standpoint to determine whether they are reasonable. Yesterday, a reporter from Dalu Daily asked the Shanghai Telephone Company about the resolution of the French Concession Municipal Council. According to an official of the company, the company did not want to express its opinion before receiving the official notification from the French Concession Municipal Council regarding the approval of charging per call.

Heavy Weight of Opium Discovered on Shanghai-Beijing Through Train, Onboard Police Received Report and Searched Back and Forth, Criminal Fearing Guilt Escaped Mid-Journey

Yesterday morning, the Shanghai-Beijing through train No. 301 on the Beijing-Shanghai Railway received a secret report from Pukou Station of the Jinpu Railway when it departed from Beijing, stating that a drug trafficker disguised as a passenger boarded the train in Xuzhou, carrying a heavy weight of opium, and requesting a strict investigation. Dong Guangrui, the police officer on duty, heard the news and, considering that the case involved drug trafficking, searched back and forth. Unexpectedly, the drug trafficker, fearing guilt, escaped mid-journey. When the train arrived at its destination, Shanghai North Station, a large number of boxes, wicker baskets, and bedding were found in the third-class carriage without anyone claiming them. Chen, the stationmaster, reported this to the North Station Police Section patrol officer Yuan Shengbiao, and they inspected the items in public. On the spot, eleven packages of opium of various sizes were found in the bedding, all packed in pillows and tightly sealed. After being weighed, it was found to be sixteen kilograms. They were immediately sent to the North Station Police Office for investigation. Zhong Jianhun, the chief of the police section, thought that there might be more concealed drugs in the large number of luggage. He and Stationmaster Chen jointly unpacked and inspected them one by one. As a result, they found that a wicker basket full of biscuits was suspiciously heavier than it should be. Upon closer inspection, they found that there was an interlayer, and four packages of opium weighing six kilograms were found in the interlayer. It is reported that the total amount of opium was twenty-two kilograms (approximately five hundred taels). The police section is indignant that such a large amount of opium dared to be trafficked from the north to Shanghai to poison the people and has decided to send it to the Songhu Garrison Command and request the arrest of the fugitive involved in the case to be brought to justice.

Central Trust Bureau Business Performance Report: Trust and Savings Deposits Reach 9 Million Yuan, Qiuhong Wharf Project to Be Completed in August-September, Central Savings Society to Open in the Near Future

The Central Trust Bureau, which opened on October 1 last year, has achieved astonishing development in its business in just three months. Its trust and savings deposits have reached 9 million yuan, the amount of insurance reaches 170 million yuan, and the insurance premium income is about 100,000 yuan. The number and amount of materials entrusted to the government by various agencies is very large, and other businesses have also achieved considerable results. Details are as follows:

Trust Business

The Bureau's trust business covers a wide range of areas. The current businesses include: Trust deposits, including current, fixed-term, and fund trusts. Because of its superior benefits and simple procedures, there are many depositors. Trust investment, including mortgage lending, purchasing securities, and depositing in banks. The Bureau uses the most reliable methods for investment in accordance with its regulations, so it can be said that the guarantee is stable. Special trust, including credit guarantee and various enterprise trusts, which has won the trust of society. Collection of money and entrusted investigation matters have also been carried out.

Savings Business

The savings of civil servants and soldiers are one of the Bureau's main businesses. The regulations on civil servant savings are currently being reviewed by the central government and will be announced soon. The regulations on military savings have already been promulgated. They have been implemented in Beijing since July last year, and various agencies, troops, and schools outside Beijing have also been ordered to implement them step by step starting from New Year's Day this year. Before the New Year, those who contacted the Bureau were constantly coming and going. Those who first sent their existing savings to the Bureau include aviation, customs, salt administration, tax police agencies, public security bureaus, and other special action teams, which are a considerable number. There are also other government agencies and public organizations that will transfer their pension and compensation to the Bureau for safekeeping and interest.

Property Insurance

The insurance of public property is stipulated in the Bureau's regulations. Since the establishment of the Bureau, the National Government has ordered all agencies to handle insurance through the Bureau. The insurance department of the Bureau has already handled the following: Property insurance, including fire insurance, water insurance, car insurance, etc. Personal insurance, including life insurance, personal accident insurance, etc. Insurance business in important places in the country is handled by the Bureau's local agencies separately. The agencies that have already insured their property with the Bureau include the Central Bank, the Ministry of Railways, the Ministry of Communications, the Postal Bureau, the State-owned China Merchants Bureau, the Supervisory Audit Office, etc. Other agencies are also contacting one after another. Starting from this year, all insurance will be handled by the Bureau.

Qiujiang Wharf

This matter was originally handled by a design meeting. After the establishment of the Bureau, it was reorganized into the Qiujiang Wharf Construction Committee, which plans all affairs of the wharf. The Qiujiang Wharf Affairs Office was established in the Bureau's Trust Department to handle the matter. The things that have been done before the New Year include: Bidding for the construction of wharf warehouses, which has been contracted by the Innovation Factory. Construction is now underway. A total of three installments of construction fees have been issued, totaling more than 460,000 yuan. Requisitioning more than 272 mu of land for the Kunlian Wharf. In addition to the more than 258 mu that have been requisitioned, a total of 190,352 yuan has been paid in compensation. There are also subsidies for demolition, relocation of graves, and agricultural losses. The mud-filling project of the wharf and the raising of the requisitioned land are being handled separately by the Bureau's entrusted dredging and dredging avoidance. The construction of Wujin Road has been agreed upon by the dredging avoidance and the Shanghai Municipal Government and will begin construction soon. It is reported that the wharf project is expected to be completed in August and September this year. This construction is closely related to the prosperity of the central area of Shanghai.

Establish Savings Society

In addition, the Bureau has been specially approved by the government to establish a Central Savings Society. Because the procedures are more complicated, the preparations have not been completed before the New Year. However, after the Bureau was ordered to take over the savings of various banks and societies, it actively reorganized them. The review of the assets and liabilities of the Sino-French Savings Society has been completed, and the original Sino-French depositors are being registered by the Bureau. It will be completed soon. The review of the assets and liabilities of the China Industrial Bank has also been completed. It is reported that another charter will be announced to the depositors in the near future. The Society will also open in the near future. The internal organization of the Bureau is also becoming perfect. All internal and external regulations have been formulated. Accounting, documents, cashier, personnel, and other items are handled in accordance with the latest system. It is reported that the final accounts for the end of the year will be completed on the same day. The total profit from the start of business to the end of the year, a total of three months, is about 80,000 yuan.
