Ministry of Finance Strictly Prohibits Handmade Cigarettes, Deregistration to Be Revoked in Four Stages Starting from January This Year, Complete Prohibition by April 1937

In order to maintain cigarette tax revenue, the Ministry of Finance strictly prohibits handmade cigarettes and has submitted a request to the Executive Yuan to order the provincial and municipal governments to earnestly assist in the investigation and prohibition of handmade cigarettes. The Ministry of Railways has also been ordered to order the railway bureaus to pay attention to prevention and confiscate smuggling. The Ministry of Railways has already ordered its subordinate railway bureaus to comply. The original report of the Ministry of Finance is as follows: (Omitted above) Since the cigarette tax was changed to a unified tax and the tax rates have been increased several times, the revenue has increased sharply. In recent years, the unified tax has been the largest source of central revenue, second only to customs and salt taxes. Cigarettes account for an important part of the unified tax revenue. Military and government expenses rely on its maintenance. The ability to achieve this result depends entirely on the centralization of production and on-site collection of taxes. According to the unified tax regulations, off-site production and sales are strictly prohibited. Handmade cigarettes can be made anywhere, are scattered and difficult to manage, and are difficult to prevent from being privately manufactured and sold, which directly hinders tax revenue and indirectly affects military and government expenses. It is extremely serious. It was originally intended to be completely prohibited, but in order to maintain the current livelihoods of the poor in the nearby regions that produce smoked tobacco, the area was identified and temporarily approved for registration, declaring that it was limited to personal self-manufacture and local sales, and was not allowed to be transported to other places, in order to crack down and avoid proliferation. On the one hand, the Ministry is currently formulating a method for phased prohibition, which will be announced and implemented. All registered cigarette households should revoke their registration by drawing lots every four months starting from January 1936, until complete prohibition by April 1937, so that they have room to change careers. This is to sympathize with the personal livelihood of the poor and cannot be discussed in the same way as the ordinary cessation of business. The manufacturing of smoked tobacco in the smoked tobacco producing area that has been approved for registration must be phased out. In addition, households that have not registered and are privately manufacturing are of course absolutely prohibited, and the people of each province are taking advantage of the opportunity of increased cigarette tax rates, and handmade cigarettes have low profits and heavy profits. Knowing that private cigarettes violate the ban, they still follow suit. In addition to the designated area, non-tobacco producing areas are also engaged in private cigarette manufacturing and sales. The spread is extensive, and even in the remote towns and villages of Jiangsu and Zhejiang provinces, there are local bullies everywhere, and some are engaged in large-scale iron machine handmade private cigarettes for profit. There are even those who falsely use the name of the military to protect private transportation, so that private cigarettes are becoming more and more rampant, and machine-made factory cigarettes are becoming more and more stagnant. This has been particularly evident in recent months. If we do not seek remedy urgently, we are sincerely worried that the situation will continue to deteriorate. In addition, the current cigarette unified tax rate is 160 yuan for the upper level and 81 yuan for the lower level per 50,000 cigarettes in a box. At this time of market decline, manufacturers pay this heavy tax and barely manage to support themselves, relying entirely on the fairness of the unified tax system. Since the country levies heavy taxes, it should take care to maintain and pay attention to investigation and suppression. If handmade private cigarettes are allowed to proliferate, not only will manufacturers justifiably criticize and be unable to cope, but in fact, heavy-tax factory cigarettes are impossible to compete with tax-free private cigarettes. If this continues, legitimate manufacturers will one day be unable to maintain themselves, and if the unified tax system is shaken as a result, the original income will inevitably be sharply reduced, and the military and government expenses that should be paid will also be a problem. Thinking about the future, I am very worried. I have repeatedly issued orders to my subordinates to strictly investigate and prohibit them. However, handmade private cigarettes are scattered everywhere, and there are not many officials in the collection agency, and their eyes and ears are difficult to cover everything. If the local administrative agencies do not assist in the investigation and prohibition, it will be difficult to achieve results. After repeated consideration, I can only ask the Executive Yuan to order the provincial and municipal governments to order the local administrative leaders in their jurisdiction to strictly prohibit private cigarette manufacturing and prevent it from spreading, and to instruct each county to include the investigation and prohibition of handmade private cigarettes in the Baojia regulations. If found, they should be held jointly and severally liable for punishment, so that everyone knows that private cigarette manufacturing violates the law and discipline, and can completely eradicate the roots to maintain the source of taxation. The handmade wooden machine cigarettes in the smoked tobacco producing areas near Shandong, Henan, and Anhui provinces, except for iron machines that are absolutely not allowed to manufacture cigarettes and should be seriously investigated and suppressed, should be limited to the cigarette households that have been temporarily approved for registration, and can only be transported and sold locally, and must not be transported to other parts. They will still be phased out by drawing lots. In addition, the manufacture of handmade cigarettes is not allowed to comply with the original plan. Attached is a list of the smoked tobacco producing areas in the three provinces of Yu, Lu, and Wan, as well as a list of the Qing Dynasty wooden machine handmade cigarette households approved for registration, which I would like to send with the document for inspection. At the same time, I request the Executive Yuan to order the Ministry of Railways to order its subordinate railways to pay attention to the prevention of handmade cigarettes, and to confiscate them, and at the same time to start the Military Commission to order the local defense forces to assist in the investigation and suppression at any time, so as to stop private manufacturing. The country's future is deeply beneficial. I have presented the reason for the proposed order to strictly prohibit private cigarette manufacturing, together with a copy of the table and book, to the Executive Yuan for consideration and implementation, and I beg for instructions to follow. I am eagerly waiting for orders.

In recent years, due to economic panic and natural and man-made disasters in our country, the increase in the number of unemployed people has aroused serious concern among the people. Establishment of the China Seamen's National Salvation United Association

Chinese seamen's organizations, in order to expand their organizations and increase their strength, have established the China Seamen's National Salvation United Association. At the founding congress, key personnel were elected, and a declaration and constitution were issued, which are described below:

Constitution

Constitution of the China Seamen's National Salvation United Association: (Name) The name of this association is the China Seamen's National Salvation United Association. (Address) The temporary address is Room 505, 5th Floor, Flour Exchange, Min Guo Road, Shanghai, c/o China Marine Engineers' Association. (Purpose) The purpose of this association is to connect seamen's organizations, carry out national salvation work, assist the government, and ensure the integrity of the nation's territory and sovereignty. (Membership) Any Chinese seamen's organization that has been reviewed and approved by the executive committee of this association may become a member of this association. (Organization) 1. Representative Congress: Representatives from each seamen's organization (two responsible representatives) form the Representative Congress, which resolves the guidelines for national salvation work. 2. Executive Committee: Elected by the Representative Congress from seven organizations, it implements the resolutions of the Congress. 3. Standing Committee: Elected by the Executive Committee from three organizations, it handles routine association affairs. 4. The Executive Committee has three sections: General Affairs Section, responsible for documentation, accounting, and communication; Propaganda Section, responsible for national salvation propaganda; and Organization Section, responsible for liaison with various organizations. 5. Special committees may be established as necessary for the work. (Meetings) The Representative Congress is convened by the Executive Committee. The Executive Committee meets every two weeks, and the Standing Committee meets weekly, convened by the chairman. (Funding) 1. Each organization pays ten yuan as stipulated. 2. Special expenses are shared equally by each organization when necessary. (Supplementary Provisions) This constitution shall be implemented upon approval by the Representative Congress. Any omissions shall be amended by the Representative Congress.

Declaration

(Omitted above) Now, Yin Rugeng has openly rebelled, severing himself from the nation. Throughout history, those who have sought foreign assistance have invariably destroyed their own country. The disasters caused by the Uyghurs and Tartars are clearly recorded in history. If we continue to tolerate and indulge, the "Ronin" [Japanese vagrant] can manufacture public opinion, and the Chinese traitors can be treated as honored guests, using the name of economic cooperation to carry out dumping and invasion, with countless conspiracies, shocking the entire country. This time, students in Beiping witnessed the situation and were heartbroken, rising up to save the country, only to be massacred by military police. Students across the country responded, appealing and marching, but North China remains as precarious as a pile of eggs. The pace of aggression is accelerating. The losses and pain suffered by the seamen's organizations affiliated with this association under these humiliating circumstances are unspeakable. Companies in the north are on the verge of bankruptcy, the number of unemployed is increasing daily, and crew members sailing to the Northeast are subjected to abuse. Before the country is broken, the home is gone; before the person dies, the heart is dead. Looking to the future, we cannot help but shudder. In this time of crisis, it is believed that only the unity and rise of all the people of the country can find a way out for the survival of the nation. It is especially hoped that the government will lead the people of the whole country to work together to save the crisis. After deliberation by the congress, the following demands are made to the people and government of the country: Oppose the nominal autonomy of North China in order to preserve the absolute integrity of territorial sovereignty, and punish Yin Rugeng, who seeks foreign assistance and willingly harms the country. Make public Sino-Japanese diplomacy and clearly announce the agreements that have been signed. Support patriotic movements, release arrested students and citizens, and severely punish the culprits. Open up freedom of assembly, association, and speech for the people, and abolish censorship of the press.

Rice and Wheat Grading Group Collects Over 300 Kinds of Wheat; Rural Economies Across Regions are Panicked

According to the Guo Wen News Agency, the Shanghai Commodity Inspection Bureau previously found the grades of rice and wheat in our country to be extremely mixed. It specifically added a rice and wheat grading group to the bureau to handle grading matters. The group is now officially operating and has stipulated that the first year's work will be a "wheat grading year." A month ago, it dispatched rice and wheat specialists Wang Zhengchao, Zhou Fengming, etc., to various counties in Jiangsu Province to collect various types of wheat for use as specimens for research. The reporter met with Wang Zhengchao, a specialist from the group, yesterday. Mr. Wang had just returned from the counties and said that after leaving Shanghai at the end of November last year, he first went to Nanjing, and then to Jurong, Zhenjiang, Danyang, Changzhou, Wuxi, Yixing, Jiangyin, Suzhou, Changshu, Wujiang, and other counties, obtaining more than 300 kinds of wheat samples. Among them, the "Wuxi Longshan Huang," "Changshu Longsui Baike," and "Suzhou Zipi" are the most famous. The distribution centers for wheat in Jiangsu Province are Zhenjiang, Lvcheng, Benniu, Qishuyan, Wuxi, Suzhou, etc., and in Benniu alone, more than 18,000 packages (each package weighing over 100 jin by market scale) are transported daily when the new wheat is released on the market. As for the rural economy in various counties, it is very panicked, especially in Jiangning, Jurong, Zhenjiang, Danyang, and other counties. Some farmers are even running out of food. The situation is better south of Changzhou, in Wuxi, Yixing, Jiangyin, Suzhou, and other counties, but it is still much worse than in previous years. The above is only a report from various counties in Jiangnan. The counties north of the Yangtze River were collected by Zhou Fengming, who has now left Yangzhou and Funing, and has transferred to Zhenjiang to take a car to Xuzhou, Haizhou, and other places. It will take another month before he can return to the bureau. It is planned to start inspection and grading after the varieties from various places have been collected, and so on.

Cheng Haifeng Discusses the Labor Situation in Zhenjiang and Wuxi: Labor Equipment in Wuxi Factories is Relatively Complete; Zhenjiang Has Not Fully Shed the Era of Handicraft Industry

Cheng Haifeng, Director of the China Branch of the International Labor Office, personally went to Zhenjiang and Wuxi last December to inspect the labor situation. He returned to Shanghai during the New Year holiday and immediately drafted an inspection report to be submitted to the Geneva Bureau. According to a report yesterday to the New Voice News Agency reporter, the old man inspected the labor situation in Zhenjiang and Wuxi last year. He first went to Zhenjiang to contact the Jiangsu Provincial Government, and then stayed in Zhenjiang to inspect. Zhenjiang Provincial City does not have large-scale factories, and the era of handicraft industry has not completely passed. Zhenjiang has an organization of the General Federation of Trade Unions, which was established in September last year. Its future plan is to merge the past scattered trade unions into the federation to fully seek the welfare of the labor sector. Later, personnel were dispatched by the Jiangsu Construction Department to accompany him to Wuxi. There are 60 factories in Wuxi that meet the factory law, and many other small factories. Cotton spinning, silk weaving, flour, and other factories are the most numerous. The labor equipment of each factory, such as worker dormitories, is considered complete, and the working environment of the workers is also good. Regarding labor welfare, the Shenxin No. 3 Factory is the best. Trade union organization in Wuxi is not universal, and the number of female workers is slightly higher. Silk weaving factories used child labor in the past, but have recently switched to new-style machines, and child labor has been eliminated. What I felt most deeply was that the unemployment problem in Zhenjiang and Wuxi is quite serious. This problem is not only limited to Zhenjiang and Wuxi, but also felt in all the places I inspected. The only way to solve unemployment is to revive the economy. Another thing that I felt most painful was the rickshaw pullers and dockworkers in Zhenjiang and Wuxi. They work hard every day and earn very little. Their daily life is the most painful among the workers. The government authorities should have a way to relieve them, he said.

Change of Magen Road Warehouse, Free Storage Date: Arrival of Goods Changed from Seven Days to Five Days

The free storage date for goods at the Shanghai-Nanjing Railway Magen Road Warehouse was previously changed to three days for departing goods and seven days for arriving goods. The storage fee for fourth-class and below is 1.5 cents per ton for a full carload and 5 cents for every 50 kilograms for less than a full carload. Now, with the approval of the Railway Bureau by the Vehicle Department, starting from January 1, 1936, the free storage date for goods arriving at the station will still be changed from seven days to five days.

Under the Depressed Market, Sino-French Property Tax Dispute: Sino-French Asks to Reduce the Estimated Annual Rent, but the Municipal Council Fails to Understand

The houses and foundations of the Sino-French Pharmacy on Beijing Road and Ni Cheng Bridge are all self-owned and were built in 1929. After the Municipal Council appraised them, the annual rent should be 20,140 yuan. The municipal general tax is collected based on this appraisal at 14%. In July 1933, the Municipal Council re-appraised it, increasing it to an annual rent of 33,566 yuan. However, the current market is extremely depressed, and property prices have plummeted as a result. Based on this reason, the Sino-French Pharmacy requested the Municipal Council to reduce the estimated annual rent to 27,781 yuan and 83 cents, so that the payment of the municipal general tax can also be calculated based on this. However, the Municipal Council refused the request and insisted on paying the municipal general tax according to the annual rent of 33,566 yuan, resulting in an irresolvable situation. For the autumn and winter tax payments last year, Sino-French paid according to the reduced amount requested, but the Municipal Council refused to accept it. On one hand, the Tax Department of the Council appointed Lawyer Ru Bao to file a lawsuit in the First Special District Court, accusing Xu Xiaochu, the manager of Sino-French Pharmacy, of owing the autumn and winter tax payments, totaling 2,349 yuan and 63 cents in national currency, requesting a judgment ordering payment and bearing the litigation costs. Sino-French also appointed Lawyer Chen Rui to file a defense and counterclaim, requesting permission to pay a quarterly tax of 972 yuan and 36 cents according to the annual rent of 27,781 yuan and 83 cents. The reasons are briefly stated that the Municipal Council initially assessed the annual rent of the Sino-French houses at 14,400 taels, and then suddenly increased it to 24,000 taels, because the Shanghai market was frequently described as developed at that time, and Sino-French especially requested an increase in installments. However, the situation has changed drastically today. Depressed phenomena permeate the city, houses are vacant, and real estate is unattended. The trend of rent reduction is raging, and the number of cases where rent is reduced through negotiation, court mediation, or judgment is unknown. The case of Aimu Yi Primary School and others are used as a ratio, and this kind of fact cannot be concealed. Furthermore, the frequent closure of silver money shops is mostly based on the fact that real estate is unattended. Therefore, the house prices in Shanghai are very different from the past. Therefore, the request of Sino-French to reduce the rent estimate cannot be said to be without reason, and so on. The case has been opened in the First Special Court by Judge Mo Runhua for trial, and the date for sentencing has been scheduled.

The Zhan Dayou Ink Shop Property Dispute Case Has Not Yet Been Concluded: Cha Qilin Sues Zhan Yunshan and Others for Forgery of Documents; Trial Opened Yesterday; Adjourned for Retrial Due to the Absence of the Defendant

The Zhan Dayou Ink Shop on Fangbang Road in this city is a century-old shop with assets of over two million gold yuan. The owner, Zhan Daosan from Anhui, died in 1929, and the dispute has continued for years without resolution. Daosan had no children, only one daughter, who married Cha Qilin, also from the same hometown. They have one son and two daughters. The son's name is Da (9 years old), and the daughters' names are Xingxian and Hongxian. (Cha Zhan died of illness in 1932.) Since Daosan's death,

The store affairs were entirely controlled by his paternal uncle, Zhan Songling. Last year, Zhan Yunshan and Zhan Songling, paternal uncles of Zhan Daosan, filed a lawsuit in the local court requesting a judgment ordering the paternal uncle Zhan Songling to hand over the account for inspection. The third trial resulted in a ruling ordering the handover. On the one hand, Cha Qilin petitioned the civil court of the local court to confirm the inheritance of the estate of his father-in-law, Zhan Daosan. Zhan Yunshan also submitted a will established by Zhan Daosan in 1929 and a succession certificate established in April 1925, stating that Daosan had no descendants and had established his second son, Bohua, as his heir. The trial result was a ruling that the property left by Daosan would be divided equally between Cha Qilin and Yunshan's second son, Bohua. Cha Qilin refused to accept this and appealed to the Jiangsu Higher Court. Recently, Cha Qilin collected evidence and, in October last year, reported to the prosecutor's office of the local court that Zhan Yunshan, Zhan Songling, and Ji committed

Forgery of documents,

Forging seals, and Zhan Jixian, Yu Ruizhi, and others committed forgery of documents and perjury. After several interrogations by Prosecutor Ru Xiu, and after retrieving the will and certificate of Zhan Daosan from the Jiangsu Higher Court, it was determined that Zhan Yunshan and others did have the criminal suspicion of forging documents and other crimes, and a public prosecution was filed according to law. At 10:00 AM yesterday, Criminal Judge Cai Dingcheng specially opened the Third Court for trial. The defendants Zhan Yunshan, Zhan Songling, Zhan Jixian, Yu Ruizhi, and others,

Did not report

Only Zhan Yunshan appointed Lawyer Peng Yuanxun as his agent to appear in court, stating that Zhan Yunshan had not arrived due to illness, and requesting an adjournment. Judge Cai approved this, and then told Lawyer Peng that the defendant must appear in court for the next hearing in order to conclude the case as soon as possible and avoid delaying the time. Lawyer Peng obeyed. Judge Cai then questioned the plaintiff, Cha Qilin, who stated that he was 32 years old, from Huizhou, residing on Guangqi Road, and was studying. He said, "You accused Zhan Yunshan of forging the will and succession certificate, etc., and they have now been sent to the Supreme Court. However, who is the first defendant?"

Who is the heir?

He replied, "It is his second son." "Question: According to the above, how many people signed?" He replied, "There are quite a few people who committed perjury." "Question: Who is Zhan Jixian?" He replied, "He is the defendant's uncle and brother." "Yu Ruizhi is the defendant's cousin." "Question: What are you accusing Zhan Songling of?" He replied, "Because the succession certificate falsely stated that Songling's son would also receive 2/10 of the inheritance. They colluded, so I also want to accuse him." After Judge Cai obtained this statement, he ordered them to retreat and await the date of the next hearing.

A Sailboat Capsized in a Gale Outside Wusongkou; 17 People Fell into the Water; Only Two Survived

A sailboat, Wang Jinfa, from Sanhe Port, Qidong, was sailing with passengers and cargo and other goods to the old Kou River near Chongming outside Wusongkou on the afternoon before yesterday, when it suddenly encountered a sea gale, which broke the mast, causing the boat to capsize. All 17 crew members and passengers fell into the water. At the time, only two crew members, Zhu Genjiang and Wang Lilang, were able to swim to nearby beaches because they were familiar with the water, escaping disaster. The remaining 15 passengers were not seen rising and all tragically drowned. It is heard that most of the drowned people were merchants from Qidong.

Postal Worker Fraudulently Cashes Money Orders, Claiming It Was Due to His Mother's Funeral, He Took This Extreme Measure; Court Trial Concluded and Sentencing Scheduled

Shao Ping, a native of Ningbo and a postal worker at the North Sichuan Road General Bureau, was found to have privately carved a seal and stamped it on receipts and money orders to fraudulently cash and use 120 yuan from six customers, including Lu Jiufeng, Zhang Zhenjiang, Lin Wenbing, Yao Zhuoqing, Lu Junyan, and Cheng Zhiqing, from money orders sent to Shanghai from Shiying and Suzhou between November and December last year. The case was discovered the day before yesterday by Zhang Guangkui, an inspector from the bureau, who reported it to the Postmaster, who telegraphed the Hongkou Police Station to send Detective Ding Shixiang to secretly arrest Shao and detain him at the police station. Yesterday morning, he was sent to the Third Criminal Court of the First Special District Court. Lawyer Zhang Shizhu from the Municipal Council stated that the defendant said at the police station that the money orders from the six households were temporarily misappropriated, and five of them were sent back in succession, but the ten yuan sent from Suzhou by the Yao family had not been given. Currently, four customers have come to court to testify. The police station has filed a public prosecution according to Articles 320 and 321 of the Criminal Law and Article 31 of the Postal Law, requesting an investigation. The money orders and receipts were then presented for inspection. According to the customers Lu Jiufeng, Zhang Zhenjiang, and Wu, the wife of Cheng Zhiqing, all money orders, totaling 75 yuan, were sent by the defendant, and so on. Yao Zhuoqing stated that the ten yuan money order was sent to Shanghai by his son from Suzhou, but he had not received it. He only found out after his son came to Shanghai. Lin Wenbing and Lu Junyan have not arrived. According to the testimony of Inspector Zhang from the post office, it was verified that the defendant had been serving in the bureau for seven years and had misappropriated the money orders from the customers due to the death of his mother, and he could not maintain it, so he took this extreme measure, asking for consideration. Judge Jiang Shuzi ordered him to be returned to custody and scheduled sentencing for next Wednesday.

Mongolian Road: A Youth Murdered – Six Stabs to the Back and Legs

Yesterday, around 4 PM, in an open space on Mongolian Road in Zhabei, in front of the former Gengxin Stage (behind Sanxingli), a young man was suddenly attacked by thugs wielding sharp knives. He was repeatedly stabbed, covered in blood, and quickly became a bloody mess. Passersby heard cries for help and went to investigate, reporting the incident to the Mongolian Road police station. The police took the injured man to the station, but the assailants had already fled. Subsequently, the youth was sent to Pushan Hospital on Xinmin Road for treatment. The doctor examined him and found two stab wounds on his back and two on each of his left and right legs, totaling six wounds. He was immediately bandaged and underwent surgery. According to the youth, his name was Chen Xiaosanzi, 20 years old, from Funing, and he lived in a thatched shed behind the Datong Road, Zhonghua Xin Road bathhouse. He had an older brother. Today, he was ambushed and attacked near 100 Jiantou on Xinjiang Road by his enemies Xu Xiaolaohan, Li Er, and Li Zhengqing behind the Gengxin Stage. The reason for the attack was related to a loan dispute. The people who stabbed him with the knives were Xu Xiaolaohan and others. The injured man remains in the hospital, with the two back wounds being the most severe. The police station has dispatched detectives to apprehend the perpetrators and bring them to justice.

Pudong Chunjiang Road: Suspect Robbery – Forced Victim to Borrow Money After Robbery, Public Security Bureau Deems Case Suspicious

The home of Sun Jingqiang, a Ningbo native who lives at 21 Chunjiangli, Chunjiang Road, Lujiazui, Pudong and works as a coppersmith at the Xiang Sheng Iron Factory, was suddenly visited by four robbers around 9 AM yesterday. Speaking in a Ningbo accent and wielding pistols, the robbers found only three or four women at home, as Sun was at work. The women were forced into a corner and forbidden to make any noise. The robbers stole a wallet from a drawer in the room, containing 14 yuan in banknotes. Not satisfied, the robbers forced Sun's wife to go to nearby Fuxing Butcher Shop to borrow 20 yuan and to Shenyu Nanhua Store to borrow 50 yuan, for a total of 84 yuan. They then fled in different directions. When Sun returned home in the evening and learned of the incident, he immediately reported it to the Pudong Branch of the Public Security Bureau. Director Zhang of the branch, considering the case to have suspicious elements, ordered Wang Shifu, the head of the investigation team, to investigate the truth and take appropriate action.

### Mi Jingshen Sues Huang Xianyao for Defamation – Trial Held Yesterday at the Second Special Court, Huang Fails to Appear, Further Hearing Scheduled

Huang Xianyao, the second son of the late wealthy merchant Huang Chu Jiu, after discovering that his father-in-law Zhou Songqing was holding 100,000 yuan of his assets, first filed a request for mediation in the local court, which was unsuccessful. Subsequently, in the Second Special Criminal Court, he filed a private suit against his father-in-law and his father-in-law for damaging bondholder claims. After the court ordered the original documents to be retrieved from the vault at the Guohua Bank, Zhou Songqing reported Huang Xianyao to the police station for forging documents. During the investigation, Huang claimed that the documents were forged by lawyer Mi Jingshen and Wu’s family. The police department initiated a public prosecution based on this, resulting in Huang being sentenced to one year in prison and being put on probation for two years. Since Mi and Wu had left Shanghai, they could not be summoned, and the trial was suspended. Subsequently, the private suit filed by the bondholders against Huang and Zhou for damaging bondholder claims was declared innocent based on the public prosecution verdict. Some of the bondholders, including Cheng Kefan, appealed the decision. Recently, Mi Jingshen, represented by lawyers Wang Shizong and Yin Shouguang, filed a private suit in the Second Special Court against Huang Xianyao for defamation. After one hearing, which was postponed due to the absence of both parties, the details were reported in the newspapers. Yesterday at noon, Judge Qiu Huan of the Second Special Court continued the hearing in Criminal Court Two. The plaintiff, Mi Jingshen, and his lawyers appeared in court. The defendant, Huang Xianyao, claimed illness and was represented by his lawyer, Zhang Ding. According to the plaintiff, he was 49 years old, from Hang County, and formerly a lawyer, residing at 45 Ziyuan Lane, Zaxinli. In the 22nd year [of the Republic], Huang Xianyao, accompanied by Wu Jia ..., came to him to entrust him with handling the lawsuit against his father-in-law, Zhou Songqing, for ... occupying his assets, claiming to have evidence. However, he did not provide it at the time. Later, Huang came with Tang Chunsheng, handed over the documents, and signed a letter of authorization. He then sought mediation in the local court, which was unsuccessful. Huang stopped coming and did not pay the litigation fees, so the case was put on hold and no formal lawsuit was filed. The plaintiff considered the 100,000 yuan documents to be significant, so he deposited them in a safe deposit box at the Guohua Bank. The judge asked why he didn't publish a notice in the newspaper to inform Huang Xianyao. He replied that publishing a notice costs money. The judge then asked if storing the documents in a safe deposit box didn't also cost money, why didn't he send them to his family? What purpose did it serve to keep them? He replied that Huang and his family were not on good terms, and he had not revoked his authorization. It was right for him to keep them on his behalf. However, Huang falsely accused him of conspiring to forge them, so he sued him for defamation. Mi's lawyer stated in court that the documents were stored in the bank under the joint seal of the plaintiff and lawyer Wu Chengyu. Mi also stated that regarding whether the documents identified by the Westerner from the police department were credible, Huang Xianyao's statements were contradictory. The plaintiff initially went to Wu Zhiping's law office to verify that the handwriting on the documents was genuine. The plaintiff's lawyer further stated that Huang Xianyao's statements and submissions in both the public and private lawsuits were highly relevant and requested that the case files be examined. The defendant's lawyer stated that the lawsuit concerned defamation and that the plaintiff should not involve extraneous matters to avoid disputes. Judge Qiu continued the questioning. Since the plaintiff, Mi Jingshen, had been prosecuted by the police department for forging documents, the court immediately ordered a bailiff to notify Judge Li Changnian, who was handling the public prosecution case, that Mi had arrived in court. Judge Li stated that the authority for the public prosecution case belonged to the police department and made no further comment. The court then ordered that the case be adjourned to the 15th to allow the defendant to appear, summon witnesses, and conduct further questioning before adjourning the court.

Aviation Donation at Concession Dance Halls Still to Be Gladly Paid by Dancers

Regarding the Shanghai office of the China Aviation Association collecting aviation donations at dance halls in the Public Concession, the method has been changed. The donations are no longer collected at the entrance but are added to the bill. The amount of the donation to be paid by the dancers at each dance hall is specified. According to the authorities of the Public Concession, the authorities have no objection to the collection of the aviation donation. However, the collection procedure should still be based on the principle that dancers voluntarily contribute and avoid any form of coercion. The collection of aviation donations at dance halls began in mid-August of last year. Prior to that, the Aviation Association sent a letter to the Public Works Department for support. The Public Works Department replied to the association on August 8, stating that it had no objection to the collection of aviation donations at dance halls in the Public Concession, but it must be stipulated that no coercive methods should be used and that dancers should be allowed to contribute voluntarily. The letter was signed by Mr. F. Perry, acting chief of the Public Works Department.

Gangster Claims to Be a Military Commander - Extorts Maochang Cotton Cloth Store - Sent Four Letters, the Extortion Amount Gradually Reduced to Hundred Golds - Shi Songlin Was Arrested When Taking the Money, and the Remaining Gangsters Escaped

Maochang Cotton Cloth Store at number 347 of Mingguo Road, west of Old North Gate in the French Concession, is solely owned by Ningbo native Shen Maochun (57 years old, residing at number 9 Deshengli, Bai'er Road, Nanyang Bridge). It has been established for a long time and its business is quite good. Two years ago, because of doing business with certain goods, someone threw a bomb as a warning. Before that, Shen had been kidnapped by bandits but escaped, and he had received threatening extortion letters. Recently, the store received four threatening letters from the Bandit Mountain Post Office on December 16th, 21st, 25th, and 27th of last year. The letters were written on official paper, stating that "First Army Commander Wen Ganglong" was raising military funds to strengthen his army. The letter claimed that the army's firearms and ammunition were well-stocked, but they lacked provisions and money. The letters were filled with absurd language. The first two letters demanded 500 yuan, the third halved it to 250 yuan, and the fourth reduced it to 100 yuan, demanding payment within a limited time and promising to send someone to collect it. If they refused to pay, the letter threatened to throw bombs within 24 hours. The envelopes of the four letters were ordinary, with "Commander Wen Ganglong" written on them and stamped with a seal, resembling an official document. The envelope also indicated the location as number 12 Daodeli, Beile Road, Wen Sealed etc. After receiving the letters, the store received more than ten phone calls from the gangsters, urging them to prepare the money and stating that someone would be sent with a receipt to collect it in person. The store reported the four letters to the French Concession police station, requesting an investigation. Detective Zhang Ziying, Qin Youyu, Tian Shiqing, detective Yin Baoke, and others were dispatched to investigate. They searched number 12 Daodeli, Beile Road, but found no one named Wen living there. After several days of investigation, they found nothing, so they sent detectives disguised as customers to wait inside Maochang Cotton Cloth Store. On February 2nd, at 4 PM, a middle-aged man went to Maochang Cotton Cloth Store, looking for the owner Shen Maochun, and presented a receipt for 100 yuan to collect the money. The detectives immediately arrested him and took him to the police station. The man confessed that his name was Shi Songlin, 30 years old, from Pudong, residing at number 200 Zhujiazhai, Chengdu Road, and that he had been entrusted by Wen Asan from Wenzhou to collect the money. The next day, the police station sent Shi to the Second Special Court for interrogation and detention. At that time, the police needed to apprehend the remaining accomplices, so they were unable to disclose the information. Now that the accomplices have fled and cannot be found, the case has been concluded by the police department. Yesterday morning, Judge Li Changnian of the Second Special Court, accompanied by Clerk Wang Baoxun, came to the First Criminal Court for interrogation. Attorney Gu Shouxi of the police department presented the case and filed a public prosecution for the crime of extortion under Article 346 of the Criminal Law, also presenting the four threatening letters as evidence. Then, Qin Youyu, the detective in charge of the case, reported on the arrest and investigation process. Zhang Chuncai, the shop assistant and representative of the plaintiff Maochang Cotton Cloth Store, also testified about receiving the threatening letters and phone calls. When questioned, the defendant Shi Songlin testified that on the morning of the 2nd, he was drinking tea in the first floor tea house at number 143 Dajing Road, Jiu Mu Di when he met a Wenzhou native named Wen Asan. He told him that he was unemployed and asked him to help recommend a business. Wen then invited him to room 12 of the Ruiyu Hotel at number 30 Xiafei Road, where he met the so-called Commander Wen Ganglong. The two men told him that they had arranged to borrow money from Maochang Cotton Cloth Store, had agreed to borrow 100 yuan, and handed him a receipt, instructing him to collect the money. They also told him to tell Maochang Store that the Xieda Xiang and Baoda Xiang cloth stores in Xiaodongmen had already lent them large sums of money. He did not know the details and happily agreed to collect the money. He was arrested as soon as he arrived at Maochang Store and knew nothing about extortion and had not conspired with Wen, etc. After examining the testimony, the court announced the end of the debate and scheduled the verdict for the 14th. The defendant was remanded in custody.

Smoker's Roster to Be Completed by the End of the Month - New Licenses to Be Issued and Verified, More Than 3,000 People Sent for Rehabilitation, Investigation Work Still Actively Underway

The Shanghai Public Security Bureau is compiling a roster of smokers, divided into three categories: *Poor People's License*, *Ordinary License*, and *Rehabilitation Poor People's License*. The *Ordinary License* and *Rehabilitation License* rosters will include eleven items: name, gender, age, origin, occupation, address, daily consumption, cause of addiction, license issue date, license number, and remarks. The *Rehabilitation* roster will include twelve items: name, gender, age, origin, occupation, address, smoking license number, daily consumption, date sent for rehabilitation, date of discharge from rehabilitation, name of rehabilitation hospital, and remarks. The roster is expected to be completed by the end of the month and submitted to the Municipal Government for approval and submission to the Military Governor. The Public Security Bureau originally scheduled October 1 of last year as the start date for issuing smoking licenses. According to regulations, the deadline is March of this year. On April 1st, the new rehabilitation licenses will be issued and verified. Therefore, the license renewal and verification of smokers must wait until the smoker's roster is completed before a start date can be determined. Regarding the annual reduction plan, the person in charge of the Bureau said that it would not begin to be implemented until October of this year. As of yesterday (the 7th), New Voice News reporters learned from the bureau that a detailed count of those sent for rehabilitation totaled 3,367, with 2,874 discharged after rehabilitation, and approximately 890 still undergoing rehabilitation. In order to continue eliminating the atmosphere of smoking in the city, the Bureau is still actively investigating smoking cases, with the aim of completing the anti-smoking work. No deadline has been decided upon.

Shanghai Postal Administration Notice No. 1284 states: In accordance with the request of the Shanghai Harbor Quarantine Administration at No. 2 Beijing Road, starting from the 6th of this month, all parcels imported from overseas containing used clothing must be sent by this Administration to the Harbor Quarantine Administration for disinfection before they can be delivered. Shanghai National Goods Company Hosted Banquet Yesterday to Thank All Sectors for Assisting in Revival - To Open After Auction of Inventory Is Complete

After the Shanghai National Goods Company suspended operations, Wang Xiaolai, Du Yuesheng, Zhang Xiaolin, Zhang Shouyong, Zhu Ziqiao, Xue Dubi, Zhu Meixian, and others worked to revive it. They have succeeded. The auction of inventory to repay old debts and advance funds is scheduled to begin today. After the auction is completed, preparations will be made to reorganize and reopen. Yesterday evening at 7 PM, at the Hangzhou Restaurant, Wu Zhihao and Chen Zhongfu hosted a banquet to thank the gentlemen from all walks of life who had helped with the revival. Chu Huiseng, Xue Dubi, Xu Yongzuo, Zhu Ziqiao, Zhang Shenzhi, Wu Yaqin, Yu Hualong, and others, as well as more than 50 reporters from various newspapers, attended. It was decided to organize a National Goods Revival Committee to assist the Shanghai National Goods Company and other national goods enterprises. The gathering ended at 9 PM. The reports of Wu and Chen are recorded below: Wu Zhihao reported: "Today, Zhihao and Mr. Chen Zhongfu have respectfully invited you all to attend, for which we are extremely grateful. Today is for the revival of the national goods industry. Previously, we received the full assistance of all of you, which has given us a ray of hope for the revival of the national goods industry. However, given the United States' silver policy, the outflow of domestic silver, the extreme tightness of finance, the dumping of foreign goods, and the plummeting market prices of domestic goods, industry and commerce have been greatly affected, and the closure of factories is often heard of. Moreover, in recent years, both floods and droughts have frequently occurred, people have been displaced, production has decreased, and the general purchasing power has become weak. The Shanghai National Goods Company, in this environment, although striving hard, was ultimately unable to maintain itself, resulting in the suspension of operations. Now, thanks to the strong support of all sectors and the sympathy and understanding of all creditors, we have achieved mutual assistance. Zhihao is deeply grateful and it is clear that you are doing your utmost to support national goods. We hope that you will provide further assistance in the future. We plan to organize a National Goods Revival Committee to extend to other national goods enterprises, so that domestic production will develop daily and sales will spread globally. We also hope that the government will provide protection and incentives, so that the economy and construction can be stable and move forward." Chen Zhongfu reported: "Today, Zhongfu and Mr. Zhiyi are hosting you to discuss the revival of the national goods industry, for which we are honored. Zhongfu returned from the North and first founded the China Xiexing Thermos Factory. After a year of research, the products were of high quality and the prices were low, surpassing imported goods. Later, due to the impact of the war, the entire factory suffered heavy losses, which shows the difficulty of China's national goods industry. Today, Zhongfu relies on the great efforts of all of you to assist in the revival of the Shanghai National Goods Company, as well as on your economic and planned assistance. Although I am talented and inexperienced, I will follow in the footsteps of all of you and hope for the success of the National Goods Revival Committee, so that the Shanghai National Goods Company can reorganize, recruit new shares, and achieve revival. That is what I hope you will assist with."

Tai Xibao Hospital Accepts Patients; Grand Opening Ceremony to Be Held When the Weather Warms Up

Mr. Zhang Gongquan, recognizing that hospitals and doctors in our country tend to be concentrated in urban areas, while rural areas greatly lack medical and health services, and also lamenting the high costs of urban hospitals, specially founded the Tai Jiabao Hospital (with an affiliated sanatorium and free clinic) last year. It is located at Tai Jiabao Bridge, commonly known as Shugou Bridge, near Liuhe on the Shanghai-Tai road, at the intersection of the three counties of Taicang, Jiading, and Baoshan, with convenient transportation. It can be reached in one hour by taking the Shanghai-Tai bus from the bridgehead of Wuzhen Road in Zhabei. The hospital's architecture is novel and grand, equipped with radiators and sanitary facilities, with self-supplied water and electricity. The hospital site covers fifty acres, with extensive lawns, and is only a little over two li from the coast. There are three major hospital buildings, equipped with the latest X-ray machines, artificial pneumothorax apparatus, sun lamps, electrotherapy machines, as well as operating rooms and pathological testing laboratories. Mr. Zhang is temporarily serving as the hospital director himself and has hired Dr. Hou Yunqing, formerly the chief physician at the Red Cross Hospital, Sacred Heart Hospital, and Guangdong Hospital, as the medical director. Inpatient rooms charge only four yuan per day for first-class accommodations, and other fees are only half of those charged by urban hospitals. Impoverished patients will receive free diagnosis and medication. Currently, in response to the needs of patients, it has begun accepting patients. Once the weather warms up, a grand opening ceremony will be held, and invitations will be sent to all sectors to visit.

Chen Youming's Wife Runs Away

Chen Youming, 34 years old from Nantong, residing at No. 14 Sande Lane, Jiaxing Road, Hongkou, deals in pigments and is from a comfortable family. Some years ago, Chen met a young woman named Zhuang Laosan (i.e., Chen Zhuang) in social circles. She is currently 24 years old and has a decent appearance. Chen was immediately captivated and deeply infatuated with her. They were deeply in love and soon rented a house in Sande Lane, living together as if they were husband and wife. However, Zhuang Laosan was fickle and unable to maintain marital fidelity. Soon, she relapsed and often stayed out late without returning. If Chen criticized her even slightly, she would start cursing, causing endless family disputes. Chen Youming, fearing that family scandals would be exposed, could only endure it in silence, even though he was extremely angry at the time. Who would have thought that Zhuang Laosan would not only fail to mend her ways but would instead change her former behavior, spending all day out, neglecting Chen and the family. On the 5th of this month, taking advantage of Chen's absence, she secretly returned to their residence, taking all the jewelry, clothes, 150 yuan in cash, and a savings deposit book from the Four Banks with a balance of 500 yuan, as well as a deposit book from Chen Zhengtai with a balance of 1,000 yuan, totaling over 2,000 yuan, and fled without a trace. When Chen returned home, he found the boxes and suitcases in the room overturned, with belongings scattered all over the floor. The person was long gone. After a fierce battle, he finally learned the whole story and immediately sent people to search everywhere, but it was like a stone sinking into the sea, with no news at all. Chen, having lost both his person and his property, was filled with grief and anger. He then reported to the relevant police authorities, requesting an investigation and declaring that he only wished for her to return. It is unknown whether she will return.

Shanghai's Rubber Industry (Continued)

— Edited by the China Credit Information Service

(4) Product Classification

Except for Xie Kang Factory, most factories currently focus primarily on footwear, and some even specialize solely in galoshes. In addition to galoshes, some also manufacture rubber shoes, running shoes, leather balls, rollers, hot water bottles, toys, rubber hoses, rain shoes, sports shoes, machinery parts, or medical equipment, either producing one type or several types. However, Xie Kang is unique because its management consists of key members of the local rickshaw industry. Therefore, its only product is rickshaw tires. In recent years, the rubber industry has occupied an important position in national industry. However, there are too many players in the industry, and the market is declining, leading to inevitable overproduction. If businesses in this industry can shift their focus and change their direction, developing other products, it may be a way to turn things around.

(5) Production and Sales Conditions

Estimating the production volume of rubber products is quite difficult. It cannot be based on their value because market prices have been gradually declining in recent years. The rise and fall of value figures are not sufficient to represent true production volume. Furthermore, products other than footwear have different units of measurement and vary in size and shape, lacking precise statistics. Therefore, this article will focus on footwear, as footwear is the core of rubber products. In its heyday, the industry had a daily footwear production volume of over 80,000 pairs. In May and June of this year, it dropped to 8,000 pairs per day, a tenfold difference. In terms of sales, the Yangtze River basin is the main market, followed by North China and Southeast Asia. South China is difficult to penetrate because there are manufacturing plants in Hong Kong and Guangzhou. Since June of this year, the industry has shown slight signs of recovery. By the end of July, most of the 32 out of 46 factories in the city that had stopped production had gradually resumed operations. Initially, it was because the central government's bandit suppression troops were gathering in Sichuan, creating a strong demand for running shoes. Subsequently, ball shoes became popular in Fujian, leading to a strong purchasing trend from Fujian merchants. In the past, the market had over 4 million pairs of shoes in stock. Recently, it has been less than half of that. The actual sales drive is the main reason, but the factories' tight finances and inability to stockpile inventory also play a role. Given China's large population and unlimited potential purchasing power, if the industry can be supported, strive for excellence, and find ways to increase tariffs on foreign goods to increase their costs, then the future of the rubber industry is by no means hopeless. (To be continued)

Educational News

After the Early Vacation for Universities in Peiping

Normal University to Study Education During Extraordinary Times; University Students Go to Various Places for Propaganda

(Special Dispatch from Peiping) Since the failure of the resumption of classes issue on the 4th in Peiping's education sector, the presidents of various schools have been preparing to start the vacation early. The students opposed both resuming classes and agreeing to an early winter vacation. However, since the early winter vacation and continuing the strike both meant no classes, although the names were different, the phenomenon of suspension of classes was the same. Therefore, the early winter vacation for various universities proceeded smoothly without any problems. However, schools that resumed classes, such as Peking University, saw constant disputes, and it is difficult to expect peace in the short term. During the vacation period, Normal University will study educational issues during extraordinary times, showing great potential for reforming education in North China. The Student Union and the work of various schools have not been interrupted due to the early vacation, and most are focusing on liaison and propaganda work. The situation in various areas is recorded as follows:

Vacation Dates for Various Schools: Peiping is the cultural center of China, and there are many universities. National Peking University and private Fu Jen Catholic University have resumed classes. After Peking University announced the resumption of classes on the 4th, bells continued to ring in various colleges for days, but few students attended classes. Private Fu Jen Catholic University, because it is managed by American Catholic personnel, has resumed classes today (7th) without any problems. The remaining universities have all started their vacations early. The vacation dates for the various universities are recorded as follows: National Peiping University, 10th; National Tsinghua University, 6th; National Normal University, 5th; Sino-French University, 4th; China College, 6th; Yenching University, 7th; Republic College, 7th; North China College, 7th.

Jiang Menglin Discusses Resuming Classes: When the reporter interviewed Jiang Menglin, President of Peking University, he said that the school's persuasion of students to resume classes was for the sake of the nation and the race, as well as the future of all students. Since 1919, he has been in the vortex of numerous student movements. Based on the experience gained from each movement, student movements must come to an end at a certain point. Otherwise, the result will not be satisfactory. A long-term strike is not only unhelpful to the student movement, but can also affect the solidarity among the students of various schools. When the school began to resume classes on the 4th, many students wanted to attend classes, but they did not attend due to the obstruction of the Student Union's patrol team. Therefore, the school affairs meeting gave a warning to the students who served on the patrol team. It has now been decided that regardless of the resumption of classes in other schools, this school will continue to hold classes. As for the students' intention to elect representatives to request the school to revoke the warning given to the students, it is feared that it will be difficult to do so, because school orders cannot be changed in the morning and revoked in the evening. In short, I love the country, love the race, and also love passionate students, but I cannot bear to see even greater and more shameful events played out in the future, affecting the entire educational system in Peiping. Therefore, I hope that the students can resume classes and understand our painstaking efforts.

Propaganda Work in Various Schools: Tsinghua University's bicycle team arrived in Dezhou on New Year's Day and entered Boji Yiyuan for an examination. White spots were found on Ms. Wu Han's tonsils. The students believe it is diphtheria. The bacteria have now been taken from Ms. Wu's mouth and she is resting. The entire team has decided to wait until Ms. Wu is definitely out of danger before continuing to move forward. Fifty students from Yenching University are scheduled to gather in Qinghe on the 8th to give lectures in nearby villages. More than 20 members of the Peking University Medical College rescue team went to Gu'an on the morning of the 7th to treat and expand the propaganda team. The first and second groups of the Student Union propaganda team arrived in Liulihe on the 7th, and the third group went to Gu'an. The Northeast University propaganda team performed patriotic dramas at the Longevity Temple yesterday. The plays were "The Tragedy of National Subjugation," "Killing the Enemy to Show Filial Piety," and "Street Night Scene." There were over a thousand peasant spectators. The police intervened, and the patrol team confronted them, holding on for a long time. The police left resentfully (7th).

Temple Property Dispute for Education Ends

Temple Properties Already Allocated for Education Expenses Must Not Be Retrieved

Regarding the matters of using temple properties to promote education and protecting temples, disputes have frequently occurred in various regions. With submissions from various parties and the government's decision on the measures, this matter can be considered settled. The details are recorded below:

Petition from Provincial Commissioners: Commissioners of Education from Jiangsu Province, Zhou Fohai; Shandong Province, He Siyuan; Anhui Province, Yang Lian; Zhejiang Province, Xu Shaodi; Hubei Province, Cheng Qibao; Hunan Province, Zhu Jingnong; Henan Province, Li Jingzhai, and others jointly submitted a petition to the Ministry of Education, stating that in the initial stages of promoting education in various provinces, there was often a shortage of funds. Organizers would often allocate local temple properties to cover the recurring expenses of schools, or use the buildings as schoolhouses, which were then submitted to local governments for approval and record. For decades, there were no issues, and the education system relied on this support. Using temple properties for education has a deep and long-standing history, and it should be firmly protected without any doubt. In recent years, temples in various regions have often used the "Supervision of Temples Regulations" or the individual "Management of Temples Regulations" of various provinces, misinterpreting and distorting the clauses, to litigate the already allocated temple properties, hoping to overturn the case. Some cunning individuals even take advantage of the opportunity to fuel the situation, even going so far as to transfer temple properties that have been administratively decided to be allocated to educational purposes to judicial resolution, ultimately overturning the original case. There are many such examples. If such a situation is not quickly prevented and properly remedied, the local education system will face a situation where funding is cut off or there is no school building, leading to stagnation and inability to maintain operations. This will not only cause disputes but also endanger the foundation of the schools, which will have a significant impact on the future of education. Commissioners, learning from past mistakes, find it difficult to remain silent and offer their humble opinions to the Ministry. According to the principles of laws not being retroactive, the issuance of the "Supervision of Temples Regulations" aims to supervise temples and their properties so that future dispositions have something to follow. It is thought that this regulation should not be used to standardize the properties that have already been disposed of, so as not to cause disturbances. This is in terms of laws. As for the temple properties that have already been decided to be allocated to educational purposes, they should be effectively protected. Various temple properties that have been decided to be allocated to educational purposes are related to designated uses and should be continuously maintained and not changed. If facts are disregarded and overturned at will, the established career cannot be handled, and it also greatly contradicts the country's intention to protect education. This is in terms of facts. Regarding the temple properties that have already been decided to be allocated to educational purposes, they should be effectively protected. For these two reasons, it is proposed that the Ministry forward the petition to the Executive Yuan to issue an order to all provinces that all schools that have already been established and have a record of using temple properties should be maintained as usual and not be disrupted. From now on, temple properties must still abide by laws and regulations and not be disposed of without authorization so that protecting temple properties can still imply the intention of safeguarding education. The future of education truly relies on this. Furthermore, the Commissioners would like to add that, at a time when the national compulsory education is beginning to be implemented, the central government has deeply understood the difficulties of the people, raised substantial funds, and provided separate subsidies. Local governments should also do more to solicit donations so that the great plan of compulsory education can be achieved as soon as possible. However, looking at the current social and economic situation, numerous exorbitant taxes and levies must be abolished, and the people's financial strength is unable to bear the burden. For now, the property of temples in various places can be used to provide assistance. It is proposed that from the 24th year, the provisions of Articles 5 and 8 of the "Supervision of Temples Regulations" should be strictly enforced for registration and periodic reporting. Also, in accordance with the provisions of Article 10, with reference to Article 5 of the "Regulations on Buddhist Temples Engaging in Public Welfare Charitable Undertakings," a specific amount of public welfare undertakings should be set based on the circumstances of the temples in various regions and the amount of property. During the implementation of compulsory education, these public welfare undertakings should be temporarily transferred to short-term primary schools or other local education projects so that the people's burden can be reduced and the progress of compulsory education can be assisted.

Opinion of the Ministry of Education: The Ministry of Education forwarded the situation to the Executive Yuan, stating that assets allocated for educational purposes should not be repossessed, as this would cause disputes and hinder education. From now on, the development of local public welfare undertakings should focus on education, which is appropriate. It is proposed that the Executive Yuan order all provincial and municipal governments that all temple properties that had been allocated for educational expenses before the promulgation and implementation of the "Supervision of Temples Regulations" should be maintained as before. After the implementation of the "Supervision of Temples Regulations," all temples should fulfill the registration requirements in accordance with Article 5 of the regulations. The expenses for engaging in public welfare undertakings in accordance with Article 10 of the same regulations should also focus on the expansion of local education. The proposals are appropriate in terms of law and reason. It is hoped that they will be examined and implemented.

Instruction from the Executive Yuan: The Executive Yuan instructed all provincial and municipal governments that the temple properties that had been disposed of by the provincial and municipal governments before the promulgation and implementation of the "Supervision of Temples Regulations" should maintain the status quo. The National Government had previously issued Order No. 400 on August 1931. Temple properties that had been allocated for educational expenses before the promulgation and implementation of the regulations should be maintained as before. The Ministry of Interior should promptly arrange for the implementation of temple registration in accordance with Article 5 of the "Supervision of Temples Regulations." The expenses for temples to engage in public welfare undertakings should focus on the expansion of local education. The "Regulations on Buddhist Temples Engaging in Charitable Public Welfare Undertakings" had previously been submitted by the Ministry of Interior to the Executive Yuan for approval and filing, and circulated to all provincial and municipal governments. In accordance with Article 2, Paragraph 1, of the regulations, which stipulates that original educational undertakings should be carried out for the people, there is no inconsistency with the original proposal. All provinces and cities should earnestly carry out the regulations.

Recent Developments in Provinces and Cities: After receiving the instructions from the Executive Yuan, the provincial governments have issued orders to all counties in the province to comply with the instructions and forward them to their subordinates for compliance.

World Sports News Snippets

World Marathon Runner Disqualified

Mr. Chapala, an athlete from the Republic of Argentina in South America, was the winner of the Aring Beck Marathon. After the last Rocky Mountain Games, a bronze statue of Mr. Chapala was built, which can be said to be the highest honor. Mr. Chapala is the personal secretary of the President of Argentina. Due to his participation in the competition, he was granted a year's leave to go to Berlin first, and then to work as an assistant in a pediatric hospital. He is only 24 years old, goes to bed before 9 pm every night, and gets up before 7 am, which is the norm of his daily life. In the morning, he practices gymnastics in the gym, and in the afternoon, he practices light 8,000 to 10,000 meters on the marathon track of the World Games. He once said the bold words, "No one can break his record in four years."

There is no problem for Mr. Chapala to win the championship in this competition. However, the International Amateur Athletic Federation has issued a notice stating that Mr. Chapala is already a member of a professional sports club and should immediately be suspended from his amateur competition qualification. Such a talent, now loses his amateur qualification, which is a pity.

The Leap Forward of New Track and Field Records in 1935

In 1935, the creators of new world track and field records collected totaled 26 events for men, with 29 new records and 12 equal records; for women, there were 4 events, with 13 new records and 3 equal records. These numerous records will be reviewed and recognized by the General Assembly of the International Amateur Athletic Federation this summer. For example,

The pole vault achievement is 4 meters and 40 centimeters (created by Glabaud), which is 3 inches higher than the original record on average, so there should be no objection to the review and recognition. Furthermore, the 100-meter record, which is eye-catching, is 10.2 seconds, the long jump is 8.12 meters, the shot put is 18.89 meters, the discus is 53.10 meters, the women's 100 meters is 11.6 seconds, the 200 meters is 23.2 seconds, and the discus is 47.14 meters. These excellent records cannot be said to be the ultimate human skills. This proves that the advancement of human special skills will be endless. (The rest of the items are omitted because there are too many)

The Problem of Male Female Athletes

Ms. "Aria Agoi", the world record holder for the women's 800 meters, has recently undergone surgery by a doctor, who said that she is a woman disguised as a man. This is indeed a strange story in the sports world. Those who possess both male and female external characteristics are medically known as hermaphrodites. Her surgery only sees the strengthening of men and no female appearance, then Aria Agoi is the reduction of a man. If her record exceeds the female standard and reaches the male standard, it can further prove her physical deformity. Furthermore, the new women's world records this year, the 47.14 meters in the discus by German Woman Mua Lu Man Yie, and the 11.6 seconds in the 100 meters by American Stocksfin, are only 17 years old, and have a great physique of 5 feet 11 inches in height and 150 pounds in weight, which is indeed a strange sight of young female athletes, how can it not make people suspect the truth? Moreover, the previous holder of the 800-meter record was a mother who had given birth to two children, which is rare. Also, such as the Polish athlete Conala Kojukihar, who once held the women's discus world record, has always had a super-female road that shines in the world, all of which can be said to be sexually different from Aria Agoi's first-class. However, the current interesting question is, should Aria's 800-meter record be preserved, or what? This is of course not necessary to discuss, the reporter said that it is a pity for Aria not to have a precious later life of female happiness. Ladies and gentlemen, are you all young girls like men? Children's Educational Novel

Little Men (1) (4) (6)

— Original by Louisa M. Alcott, Translated by Zheng Xiaocang

Many comrades quite agreed with Ned's conjecture, however, Mr. Bhaer was still not bad; Ned perhaps would rather confess on the spot and get this matter over with quickly, because even the most severe beating from his father was better than the indifference, avoidance, and general suspicion he encountered everywhere now. Although he was here, he was as if exiled to a deserted place; strangely enough, although no one had raised a hand to him or said a word, he had suffered deeply this week, and the days felt extraordinarily long, as if they were unwilling to pass.

The worst part was here; if they had simply said it outright, or even beaten him severely, it would have been easier to bear than the silent distrust on everyone's faces. Even Mrs. Bhaer's face showed traces of that distrust, although her behavior was still almost as kind as before; as for the worried look in Uncle Bhaer's eyes, it pierced Ned's heart, as he loved his teacher very much, and knew that his unfortunate incident had completely disappointed him.

Only one person in the whole family still had complete trust in Ned, and no matter what the opinion of everyone else was, stood bravely on his side. This was little May. She could not explain why she could overcome all the signs and still believe in him, she only felt that she could not suspect him, and her passionate sympathy made her willing to defend him without hesitation. She did not want to hear people say he was not, no matter who said it, she had indeed beaten her dear brother John, when he wanted to make her believe that Ned must have done it, because no one else knew where the money was.

Foreign Exchange in the Past Year

— Ancestral Shrine

Since the Wall Street stock market crash in September 1929, which induced a world economic panic, countries have successively abandoned the gold standard as a consistent means of saving the panic. Although there was resistance from the Gold Bloc countries, the state of their internal economic downturn seemed to prove that this trend was irreversible. Professor Cassel said, "The world economy cannot recover, which is due to the insistence of the Gold Bloc countries on the gold standard."

Abandoning the gold standard, in general terms, means inflation domestically and falling exchange rates externally. The purpose is to stimulate production and increase exports (Note 1). However, abandoning the gold standard does not necessarily mean inflating the currency immediately. If we try to examine the United Kingdom after 1931 and the United States after 1933, the number of issues is very stable, and there has been no rapid increase (Note 2). The reason is that in recent years, the departure of countries from the gold standard is different from the purpose of abandoning the gold standard during the war. During the war, the abandonment of the gold standard by various countries was for financial purposes, so it was necessary to inflate the currency (or it can be said to be its active attempt), while in recent years, the abandonment of the gold standard by various countries is intended to use the method of devaluing foreign exchange as an aid to increasing exports. The method of domestic support for industrial and commercial development is at most, and it is not necessary to increase the issuance.

If you want to devalue foreign exchange to achieve the purpose of increasing exports, you must also consider the relationship between domestic currency purchasing power and prices. In other words, you must make the purchasing power of domestic currency different at home and abroad to have the effect of promoting exports. In general, when a country devalues its foreign exchange, the purchasing power of its currency falls at home and abroad. At this time, the following three different forms may occur.

The decline in the purchasing power of domestic currency is smaller than the purchasing power abroad.

The decline in the purchasing power of domestic currency is equal to the purchasing power abroad.

The decline in the purchasing power of domestic currency is greater than the purchasing power abroad.

Among the above three situations, only in the first situation can the increase in exports be promoted, that is, devaluing foreign exchange. The decline in the purchasing power of domestic currency abroad (conversely, the increase in the purchasing power of other countries' currencies) is greater than the degree of decline in purchasing power at home. If it is the second situation, there will be no effect, and in the third situation, not only will it not promote exports, but it may expand the domestic market. (To be continued)
